More than 2,000 people, including Minister of the Navy Osumi, military councilors, naval personnel, and celebrities from the government and the public, attended. More than 100,000 people from the public watched. The Taigei ship was launched from the slipway to the music of the military band, and the ceremony ended at about 3:00 p.m. (United Press Telegram on the 16th)

Yokosuka The Japanese Navy boasted that the world's submarine tender Taigei was launched in a magnificent ceremony attended by Minister of the Navy Osumi and naval stars. The advantages of the Taigei are as follows: length 197.3 meters, width 18.04 meters, draft 5.2 meters, standard displacement 10,000 tons, speed 20 knots, horsepower 13,400, equipped with cannons, two anti-aircraft guns, four high-angle guns, and two machine guns. Its excellent performance, even compared with the famous British submarine tender Medway (15,000 tons, speed 16 knots (American submarine Holland, (11,570 tons, speed 16 knots), is clearly the world's unique warship. (Dentsu Telegram on the 14th)

(New York) Newspapers here are commenting on the British government's naval construction program. "The New York Times" believes that the British expansion of the navy is due to the tension in the Eastern Question, saying that if the military party gains power in Tokyo in the long run, European countries and the United States cannot stand idly by in the face of Japan's ambition. British competition from Japan affects India, so it has to find ways to protect its commercial and shipping interests. The United States in the Philippines is in the same situation as the United Kingdom in India. Moreover, the United States is the maintainer of the open door in China. In times of emergency, the United Kingdom and the United States rely on naval power to exert pressure on Japan. (Havas Telegram on the 16th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese military, having learned from the Kanto air defense exercises, ordered the Army Aviation Headquarters to study countermeasures to cope with the crisis in 1935 and 1936. It is reported that a draft plan has been formulated to newly establish air defense aircraft teams in major cities such as Tokyo, Kyoto, Osaka, Nagoya, Fukuoka, and the military industrial center of Kitakyushu, at a cost of 20 million yuan. Although the Ministry of the Army is well aware of the financial difficulties, it believes that air defense is an urgent matter and has decided to ask the Ministry of Finance for temporary funds again. (China United Press Telegram on the 16th)

(Tokyo) Many Japanese islands have extremely inconvenient connections with the mainland. The Ministry of the Interior ordered various departments to study connection methods and decided to adopt radio communication methods. On the 21st of this month, ultra-shortwave radio equipment will be set up on both sides of Sakata City in Yamagata Prefecture and Tobishima Island in the Sea of Japan, with both broadcasting and receiving functions. Test communication will be conducted. If the results are good, the same method will be used to connect the 21 islands under the jurisdiction of various prefectures along the Sea of Japan, such as Aomori, Akita, Yamagata, and Niigata. At a time when Russo-Japanese relations are deteriorating, this type of plan is very noteworthy militarily. (China United Press Telegram on the 16th)

(Washington) U.S. Secretary of Commerce Roper announced today the Atlantic scheduled aviation plan. The start-up funds have been allocated from the public works funds and will be prepared immediately. The estimated start-up funds are 30 million yuan. All aircraft will be purchased and operated by the U.S. government. In the future, it is planned to open daily scheduled flights between New York and major European cities, crossing the Atlantic in 24 hours. Along the way, a floating station will be set up every 500 miles on the Atlantic Ocean, equipped with repair shops and temporary lodging for passengers to prevent accidents. In the future, it is also planned to set up two rows of floating stations in the Atlantic Ocean, so that aircraft can depart from several major cities on the Atlantic coast of the United States, without being limited to New York. It is estimated that the total cost will be about 30 million yuan. Soviet Russia Makes Concessions to the United States - Freedom of Religion Can Be Recognized by Russia

(Washington) President Roosevelt and Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov met twice today. According to reliable sources, the situation is now better, and the outstanding issues between the United States and Russia are expected to be resolved. The general impression here is that Soviet Russia has agreed to discuss issues involving relations between the two countries, without making direct recognition a prerequisite for seeking understanding on such issues. It is reported that the U.S. President is now seeking an understanding that Americans in Russia have freedom of religion. According to Moscow sources, if this is the only thing hindering the United States from recognizing Soviet Russia, then this matter can be resolved quickly and Washington will be satisfied. The Russian side claims that foreigners residing in Russian cities have never experienced any difficulties in exercising their religious beliefs at present, because many churches continue to open in Russia. (Reuters Telegram on the 15th)

(Washington) The U.S. President continued to consult with Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov today. Although no official statement was issued afterwards, according to reliable sources, the resumption of relations talks has made significant progress. It is expected that the President will invite Litvinov to go to the hot springs for rest on Friday if the talks have not ended. (National Telegram on the 15th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt and Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov met at the White House before noon and after lunch. This was the first meeting between the two since the meeting on Sunday evening. Litvinov's audience with the President was not predetermined, as people generally believed that the President would only meet Litvinov after the issue of resuming U.S.-Russian relations was ready. In addition, Roosevelt told reporters that the U.S.-Russian negotiations were proceeding normally, and that even if no agreement was reached between now and Friday, or even until Monday next week, it should not be said that the Soviet Russian negotiations had failed. The President also said that his discussions with Litvinov had made progress and would continue to make satisfactory progress. (Havas Telegram on the 16th)

(Washington) The U.S. request that Soviet Russia acknowledge the debts owed by previous governments before the Russian Bolshevik Revolution is an obstacle to U.S.-Russian compromise. The United States advocates establishing a cooperative in New York to levy a surtax on U.S. goods sold to Russia to offset Russia's old debts. Litvinov is hesitant because this method would put Soviet Russia in a dangerous position with respect to other creditor nations. Roosevelt said that this surtax would be levied by the U.S. Export Trading Company (i.e., the above-mentioned cooperative), and Russia does not have to grant the same treatment to other countries. (Havas Telegram on the 16th)

The U.S. on the Immigration Issue - Revokes the Movement to Exclude Asians - Its Influence Has Expanded Greatly in Recent Months

(Washington) Dickens, a member of the House Immigration and Naturalization Committee, is carefully studying the issue of revoking the law excluding Asian nations and formulating quotas to restrict Far East immigration, paying particular attention to whether this move can win the cooperation of Far East countries and prohibit the suggestion of smuggling Eastern people into the United States. According to reliable statistics, about 8,000 Eastern people are smuggled into the United States each year, so the next meeting of Congress may consider formulating a quota plan. The movement to revoke the law excluding Asian nations has gained great momentum in recent months. What is even more surprising is that California, which originally demanded the exclusion of Eastern nations, now has a large number of supporters of this movement. (National Telegram on the 15th)

Rapid Changes in the European Situation: Germany and Poland Establish a Reconciliation Agreement; Britain Convenes a Four-Power Conference; Simon Departs for Geneva Today

(Berlin) As a result of talks between Chancellor Hitler and the new Polish Prime Minister Lipski, Germany and Poland have established an agreement. This action is significantly related to peace in Europe. According to an official statement issued after the talks, the governments of Germany and Poland have now established a complete understanding. Hereafter, all related matters will be resolved directly through negotiations between the two governments. In order to maintain peace in Europe, Germany and Poland have agreed not to resort to force in matters of negotiation between the two countries. (Reuter, 15th)

The German-Polish Declaration of Non-Aggression: A Major Factor in Stabilizing the European Situation

Warsaw All newspapers state that after Germany and Poland established an agreement, Poland's security has increased, which is of great significance even in Europe and does not harm Poland's existing allies. "The Polish News" stated that among German politicians capable of making appropriate arguments, Hitler is the foremost. "The Polish Express" stated that the Locarno Treaty failed to guarantee the security of Europe's eastern borders; the current German-Polish declaration of non-aggression compensates for this deficiency. Furthermore, economic negotiations between the two countries are proceeding smoothly. "The Polish Daily" stated that the rapprochement between Poland and Germany is the policy embraced by the Minister of Military Affairs and General Piłsudski, who personally presided over it at critical moments. This agreement is the first step in the realization of Piłsudski's policy. (Havas, 16th)

(Berlin) The semi-official Wolff News Agency yesterday released a message stating that the governments of Germany and Poland both believe that common issues should be resolved through direct negotiations, and that force should not be used in mutual diplomatic relations. Observing this message, it is clear that relations between Germany and Poland are trending toward conciliation. If negotiations indeed lead to an agreement, then a major obstacle to stabilizing peace in Europe will be eliminated. The declaration of mutual non-aggression can be seen as a precursor to the establishment of a formal treaty of mutual non-aggression, the signing of which will not be far off. Since May of this year, German newspapers have ceased to comment on the "Danzig Corridor" issue. This is a clear indication of the Hitler government's initial need for peace. The second stage of the rapprochement between Germany and Poland will necessarily involve continued negotiations to end the economic warfare between the two countries since 1914. (These negotiations began on the ninth of last month.) The Berlin Daily recently published an article stating that after Germany and Poland reach a compromise, France will be more likely to approach Germany. The reason is that France has always spoken of the need to protect its allies. Now that France's allies have established friendly relations with Germany, the need for protection will naturally decrease. (Havas, 16th)

(Geneva) It is rumored that the governments of Poland and Germany have reached an agreement in principle regarding the issuance of a declaration of non-aggression. The Disarmament Conference was both surprised and pleased by this news. Since this news originated from both Warsaw and Berlin, it certainly has the effect of easing international tensions. However, there is one condition: the spirit ostensibly displayed by the Berlin government must not be negated by facts, and must not be contradicted by the issuance of any document. French figures in Paris and Geneva do not view this news as surprising and are in fact quite pleased, as this agreement is in line with France's policy of pursuing a common European understanding. (Havas, 16th)

Britain Actively Salvages Disarmament; Has Already Contacted Various Countries Separately

(London) The government held two meetings this morning and evening to study the current disarmament situation. The British government is not only in contact with the governments of France, Italy, and the United States, but also, more importantly, is engaging with the German government in order to find a way for Germany to return to the Disarmament Conference and the League of Nations. It is heard that some cabinet members have previously advocated that preliminary talks between countries, especially between France and Germany, should take place at a location other than Geneva. There is talk of a hypothetical location in London. Outside sources speculate that the cabinet holds differing opinions on Foreign Secretary Simon's handling of the disarmament issue, but the responsible sectors do not take seriously the rumors that the Foreign Secretary will resign. (Reuter, 15th)

(London) Judging from the situation of the two cabinet meetings yesterday, the British government is determined to prevent the current disarmament stalemate from continuing indefinitely. It is widely believed that Germany has reaffirmed its goodwill through its diplomatic channels. British officials are now increasingly inclined to make practical concessions to Germany's views. Talks between the governments concerned will continue, with the primary aim of reconciling the views of France and Germany, in order to pave the way for a compromise with Germany. The meeting place for representatives of the major powers appears to be Rome, rather than London. (Reuter, 16th)

(London) The Disarmament Conference is in a deadlock. Today's cabinet meeting seeks to find a way out. If no proposals are made by foreign parties within the next few days, the British government will abandon its wait-and-see policy, which it has adopted since Germany's withdrawal from Geneva. (Havas, 15th)

(Geneva) At the last meeting of the Steering Committee of the Disarmament Conference, cabinet members from the major powers did not attend, which Chairman Henderson found very unsatisfactory. Smaller countries also hold the same view, believing that this action hinders the progress of negotiations. Representatives from Greece, Czechoslovakia, the Netherlands, Norway, and Poland originally intended to jointly issue a declaration in support of Henderson. However, these representatives have now decided to urge Henderson to consult with the Vice-Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Politis (Greece), and the Czech representative Beneš, to jointly issue a statement to all members, drawing their attention to the need for the major representatives to remain in Geneva in order to advance the work of the Disarmament Conference. (Reuter, 15th)

A Four-Power Conference Will Open in Rome

Simon Departs for Geneva Today

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon and Under-Secretary Eden will depart for Geneva tomorrow to discuss with Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson the matter of reconvening the Disarmament Conference. The British Cabinet has resolved to convene a Four-Power Conference in Rome to exchange views, in the hope of concluding a disarmament convention. Rome is widely seen as a natural meeting place, as Germany is unwilling to return to Geneva. However, France favors Geneva, which is a major difficulty. It is heard that regardless of what happens in Geneva, the British government still considers its draft convention to be the basis for all future work. Furthermore, Geneva will discuss the possibility of convening a conference of signatory states to the Four-Power Convention. (Reuter, 16th)

(London) British Foreign Secretary Simon and Under-Secretary Eden have decided to depart for Geneva on Friday. Today, Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson spoke at length with the two men via long-distance telephone, strongly arguing for the necessity of chief representatives to attend the Steering Committee meeting on the 24th, and urging the two to set out on their journey. It is also heard that the two will urge French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour to travel with them when they pass through Paris. In addition, it is heard that Henderson has also requested the Italian chief representative to attend the Steering Committee meeting, as Henderson still hopes to salvage the collapse of the Disarmament Conference. (National Telegram, 16th)

France Tentatively Approaches Germany; Says Saar Issue is Negotiable

(Paris) Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour's speech in the Chamber of Deputies yesterday will be printed in pamphlets and distributed to the governments and foreign affairs committees of parliaments of various countries. Responsible officials state that, from France's perspective, the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference still exist, and all diplomatic actions should still have Geneva as their destination. The recent wavering attitude of Britain towards the Disarmament Conference, and Mussolini's criticism of the League of Nations by Italy, cannot change France's attitude. Furthermore, the misunderstanding between Italy and France has been resolved, and the points agreed upon by Britain, the United States, France, and Italy at the end of September remain the same. From these two perspectives, we can still have some hope. The difference between French and Italian views lies in the international organizations in Geneva. Paul-Boncour's stance is to always trust the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference, while Italy wants negotiations between several strong countries to replace the various international conferences attended by all countries of the League of Nations. Such is the difference. As for the possibility of direct negotiations with Germany, the general principles held by France remain consistent: Germany proposes a plan, and then it is studied and discussed using diplomatic means, based on the spirit of international cooperation and coordination. For example, regarding the economic relations of the Saar region, negotiations can begin from now. If the people of the Saar vote in 1935 and decide to cede the Saar to France or return it to Germany, then this matter will become a purely Franco-German issue. In addition, responsible officials also stated that Franco-Russian relations have been fully improved, and France has sent technical commissioners to Soviet Russia to replace the German technicians who have been dismissed. (Havas, 15th)

French Newspapers Reveal Secret German Documents; Claim Germany Wants to Drive a Wedge Between British and French Relations

(Paris) It is heard that the German government has sent instructions to its representatives and secret operatives in North and South America, instructing them on how to conduct anti-French propaganda. These secret documents were published today by the "Le Petit Parisien" newspaper here. According to the report, "France is Germany's irreconcilable enemy." As for Britain, it is "France's strongest ally and the most dangerous to Germany. Therefore, Germany should diplomatically strive to disrupt relations between these two countries." The document discusses Germany's views on world policy, stating that "Germany, no matter what, must achieve the goal of revising the peace treaty. Germany's demands are roughly as follows: (1) All territories with German minorities must be returned to Germany. (2) Germany's former colonies must be straightforwardly returned to Germany. (3) Germany should obtain genuine equal rights in armaments and reject any international arms control system. It is naturally difficult to fulfill these demands, but Germany has no other option at present. In this matter, world public opinion is very important, so the German government is determined to sacrifice huge amounts of money to gain the sympathy of world public opinion." "Le Petit Parisien" stated that the above is the principle of German propaganda, and the methods it uses will be announced later. (Havas, 16th)

Britain Approaches Us; Conservative Party Members Advocate Moving the Embassy South

(London) The London Times today published a letter from Conservative Member of Parliament, Mr. Lunn, stating that Britain should end the isolated status of the British Embassy in Beijing, and that the British Ambassador should have a residence in Nanjing or Shanghai, so that he can reside in Nanjing or Shanghai for six months each year. Lunn also mentioned the emptiness of the House of Lords' discussion of this matter on November 8, stating that if our policy is to be effective, it must be judged based on the facts seen by the British Ambassador in China, and cannot be imagined from 10,000 miles away, and the British Ambassador must have close contact with important figures in Nanjing, in order to achieve its purpose, and cannot be blindfolded, groping for news in the dark, and indirectly forming its conclusions. Britain Rejects Japanese Goods

US Treasury Secretary Woodin Retires

Roosevelt Appoints Morgenthau as Acting Secretary

Initial Victory for the Inflationist Faction

(Washington) The first crack in the Roosevelt government has now appeared. It was learned today that Treasury Secretary Woodin submitted his resignation several days ago. President Roosevelt has decided to grant him a leave of absence. The so-called leave of absence is purely a face-saving measure. President Roosevelt is now in fact the master of the Treasury Department. Although he has appointed Morgenthau, the director of the Farm Credit Administration, as Acting Secretary, Morgenthau will not hold back President Roosevelt. Undersecretary of the Treasury Acheson also resigned. Currently, Morgenthau is temporarily serving as both Secretary and Undersecretary of the Treasury. Officials say that Acheson voluntarily resigned to make way for Morgenthau, but non-official sources say that Acheson resigned in opposition to President Roosevelt's monetary policy.

Differing Political Views Lead to Leave of Absence

Although rumors that Woodin and Acheson intended to leave the Treasury Department have been circulating for many weeks, they suddenly became a reality today. People in Washington were shocked, as if struck by lightning from a clear sky. According to President Roosevelt's announcement, Woodin will be on leave starting at the end of this week.

When the Senate investigated the business of Morgan Bank, it implicated Woodin, pointing out that Woodin was one of those who became wealthy by following the advice of Morgan and others to engage in speculative activities. At the time, many expected Woodin to resign because of this, but Woodin still did not leave.

Woodin has recently been suffering from a throat ailment and has been regularly treated by specialists. He submitted a letter of resignation several days ago, but President Roosevelt did not accept it, but instead asked him to temporarily put aside all administrative matters and concentrate on recuperating. Hence, today's announcement of Woodin's leave of absence. However, once Woodin leaves, he will not return.

London is very concerned about the new developments in Washington today, because Woodin and Acheson were both advocates of sound money. If they do not hold the reins of finance, it is feared that monetary policy may deviate from the right track.

The fact that the price of gold in the United States has not changed has made the US dollar show some improvement today. The British Exchange Equalization Fund is no longer used to maintain the gold standard, but the trend of competing to buy pounds has surged again. In addition, the news from Washington that the Treasury Secretary has changed has made the US dollar weaken again, reaching a new low of one pound equaling five US dollars, forty-one and a half cents.

Morgenthau is the son of the former US Ambassador to Turkey and is only forty-two years old. He is relatively young among cabinet members. He was educated at Cornell University and later entered the publishing industry. During the war, he served in the Navy and followed President Wilson for many years. He served as chairman of the New York State Agricultural Advisory Board. (Reuter, 15th)

Strange Cold in the US Freezes Dozens to Death; Japanese Cargo Ship Aground, Suffers Heavy Losses

(New York) The United States is experiencing a strange cold, which has already frozen twenty people to death. Pennsylvania has experienced a record snowfall of 41 inches. The poor weather has affected navigation. Storms have swept through the Great Lakes at speeds of 40 miles per hour, causing two cargo ships to run aground and two others to be damaged. A Japanese cargo ship ran aground at the port of Chiminas in Canada, and it is reported to have suffered heavy damage. Snow covers the ground everywhere in the Midwest, and the weather is very cold. (Reuter, 16th)

Acting Secretary Supports Gold Purchase

(New York) Morgenthau announced his firm support for President Roosevelt's policy of buying gold at home and abroad in the hope of raising prices. According to the New York Sun, Morgenthau advocated halving the gold content in the US dollar and opposed stabilizing the exchange rate early. The first split in President Roosevelt's cabinet is seen as a setback for the sound money faction. Rumors are now rife, with some saying that government officials have differing opinions, and others saying that Treasury Department advisor Sprague and Federal Reserve Bank President Black will both resign. Wall Street does not pay much attention to the resignation of Woodin and Acheson, but believes that this is the initial step in the inflationist faction's active pursuit of its monetary movement. (Reuter, 16th)

(Washington) It is learned that there will be further changes in important personnel in the Treasury Department. Although Woodin solemnly stated in his letter of resignation that the Treasury Department fully supports the President's monetary policy, it is widely rumored that Woodin has always opposed this experiment. It is also said that Treasury Undersecretary Acheson also disagreed with the monetary policy, so he resigned when Woodin took leave. It is also heard that Woodin's assistant, Klemmer, will also resign from the Treasury Department soon. Treasury Financial Advisor Sprague, a former advisor to the Bank of England, has always opposed expanding the currency to save the low price of goods. He is also seriously considering the issue of resignation. In addition, the position of President of the Federal Reserve is said to be vacant soon, but the current President, Black, is only temporarily in office. (National Telegram, 50th)

Monetary Doubts Are Becoming Increasingly Strong

(New York) The doubts about currency in the securities market for several weeks have become increasingly strong today due to the sudden change of senior officials in the Treasury Department. People in Wall Street explained that Woodin's leave, Acheson's resignation, and Morgenthau's taking office were all concessions made by the US government to the inflationist faction. Because Woodin has always been recognized as the leader of the sound money faction in the Treasury Department in the monetary war in Washington, and Morgenthau has always been known for his tendency to inflate the currency. Therefore, people in Wall Street believe that this change will not hinder the progress of suppressing the gold dollar. (National Telegram, 15th)

The Shock at Home and Abroad is Very Strong

(New York) President Roosevelt wants to give his gold plan a complete experiment, supplemented by sympathetic officials, and will not allow others to obstruct it. Washington dispatches from newspapers here claim that President Roosevelt is the most agile and scheming political strategist in the United States.

Acheson, who has now resigned from his position as Undersecretary of the Treasury, stated today that not only does he have doubts about the appropriateness of the gold plan, but also those who remain in office due to President Roosevelt's personal feelings have the same doubts as him. Acheson is a friend of bankers such as Morgan, and the bankers accuse the Financial Rehabilitation Agency of illegally buying gold. Morgenthau, the current Acting Secretary of the Treasury, is a close friend of President Roosevelt, and he studied under Professor Warren, President Roosevelt's trusted advisor.

Officials have not yet commented on yesterday's developments, but Senator Harrison said that inflation will be realized in an instant, and Senator Thomas said that when the value of the US dollar is halved, it can be stabilized by international agreement, and the remainder will be used as the basis for expanding the currency. Wall Street is now silent. A financial reporter for the New York Telegraph said that our monetary policy is now advancing towards destroying the credit of our currency assets and investments. There is no hope of stopping the outflow of US dollars until our gold policy is completely abolished.

The liquidation of the Morgan Securities Group is widely believed to be evidence that Wall Street is concerned about inflation. It is rumored that the United Kingdom is now considering temporary emergency legislation in order to block the outflow of funds from the United States. After this news was transmitted, the outflow of US dollars accelerated. The New York American reported that the current state of the US dollar's actions may not be an indication that the gold policy is powerless, because the Financial Rehabilitation Agency can sell gold abroad and recover a large number of US dollars. British Deputy Finance Minister Ross has now set off to return home, expressing pessimism about the possibility of resolving the war debt and the future of American finance. (Reuter, 16th)

Britain and France Are Most Anxious

(London) Business circles in London are all concerned that a low US dollar may have an impact on suppressing the value of the pound. However, the fact that British railway revenue is still high and trade is also expanding can still be comforting. Silver trading seems to be purely speculative. The United States is freely selling in the London market on the one hand, and vigorously buying in New York on the other hand. A Washington dispatch from the Times says that President Roosevelt is determined to dominate the international gold market, not only wanting to raise prices in the United States, but also in all parts of the world. There is no doubt about this. However, the continued decline in US government bonds and the impact on European currencies will eventually prevent President Roosevelt from achieving his goals. US prices have not yet responded to President Roosevelt's policies. (Reuter, 16th)

(Paris) The dismissal of US Treasury Secretary Woodin is seen as a victory for the advocates of currency inflation, because the monetary faction sees Woodin as the stopper of their ambitions. The financial markets were not affected by Woodin's resignation. The French are quite concerned about the United Kingdom's actions in maintaining the currency price with the equalization fund, because the stability of the pound is even more related to France than the stability of the US dollar. (Reuter, 16th)

Satisfied with the Implementation of the Gold Purchase Policy

(Washington) The White House stated that the US President feels satisfied with the implementation of his gold purchase policy, so he does not intend to change the plan at present. Today, the monetary issue has been temporarily put aside, and attention has been turned to unemployment relief. The President urged the governors, mayors, and local relief directors who came to the White House to fully cooperate with the central government's plan to employ 4 million people within one month, and solemnly stated that the government does not intend to gain any political benefit from this relief plan. (National Telegram, 15th)

(Washington) General Johnson, the executor of the National Recovery Act, has now reported to the US President that the provisions in the rules of the Recovery Act for increasing work and placing the unemployed are not fully complied with and must be strictly enforced. (Reuter, 15th)

Huge Fraud Case in London; Merchant Harman Sentenced to 18 Months in Prison

(London) The case in which Harman and other directors of the Korea Society were accused of fraud in transactions with Japanese subsidiary companies in order to deceive shareholders has been finalized today. The jury found that Harman had committed 21 of the crimes listed in the indictment, so the judge sentenced him to 18 months in prison. Cornelius Lev was convicted of conspiracy and sentenced to six months in prison, but was pardoned. The chairman of the society, Pons, and Zhang Ge were found not guilty and acquitted. The protagonist of this case is very famous in the history of the City of London, because Harman started as a clerk, and the companies he manages today have a total capital of 14 million British pounds. The businesses involved include rayon, gold mines, oil, rubber, and brewing. A few years ago, he bought Lundy Island in the English Channel for 16,000 pounds, minted coins, printed stamps, and promulgated laws on the island, so he was once given the title of uncrowned king of Lundy Island. Later, the government considered Harman's minting of coins to be illegal, and Harman lost sovereignty over the island. Harman originally planned to go to the Far East in March of this year to inspect the industries of the Korean Conference, but was unable to do so due to his arrest. (Reuter, 15th)

Radio Inventor Marconi and His Wife Arrive in Japan; To Arrive in Shanghai from Dalian on the 27th

(Tokyo) Radio inventor Marconi and his wife arrived in Yokohama at 12:40 PM today aboard the Chichibu Maru. Before arriving at the port, the Marquis first used the Chichibu Maru's radio, and exchanged greetings with radio scholars welcoming him via the shortwave invented by the two. Those welcoming him at the port included officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Communications, the Broadcasting Bureau, and numerous scholars studying radio. The Marquis and his wife disembarked amidst the welcoming voices and went to the Imperial Hotel in Beijing. Tonight, they will attend the welcome banquet held by Kihachiro Okura at the Koyo-kan in the Shiba district. Tomorrow, they will enter the palace to pay their respects to the Emperor. Because the Emperor is currently in mourning, they will register and leave. They will then visit the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Army, Navy, Communications, and Railways. As envoys of the Roman Pope, they will visit the Italian Embassy in Japan. In the afternoon, they will attend the luncheon hosted by Foreign Minister Hirota. At 4:00 PM, they will attend the ceremony to install him as Honorary President of the Institute of Electrical Engineers. On the 18th, they will tour Nikko. On the 19th, they will depart from the Imperial Hotel at 10:00 AM and tour Hakone. On the 20th, they will tour Kyoto. On the 21st, they will visit Nara. On the 22nd, they will visit Osaka to enjoy the autumn colors of Japan. On the 23rd, they will take a connecting ship from Shimonoseki to Keijo (Seoul). On the 24th, they will tour Keijo. On the 25th, they will go to Shenyang. On the 26th, they will go to Dalian. They are scheduled to depart for Shanghai from Dalian on the 27th. (Electric Communications, 16th)

He Yingqin Arrives in Tianjin, Holds Banquet for Jin Yunpeng, Sun Chuanfang, etc., Hoping to Jointly Eliminate the North China Crisis

Tianjin Correspondence: He Yingqin, Chairman of the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission, arrived in Tianjin yesterday (the 13th) at 11:20 AM, accompanied by his wife, as well as Liu Duoquan, Song Zhenqu, Zhu Shiqin, Chang Jingwu, advisors to the Military Branch, and Tao Shangming, commissioner of the Luanshu Administrative Office. Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong led Wei Jian, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Chen Baoquan, Director of the Education Department, Mayor Wang Tao, Ning Xiangnan, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and others to welcome him at the train station. When the special train arrived, security personnel provided special protection, prohibiting unauthorized persons from entering the platform. After the train stopped, He Yingqin alighted, and Yu Xuezhong and others approached the train to greet him. They then rode together in automobiles to the provincial government to rest. Immediately, a banquet was held at the provincial government, with the directors of various departments in attendance. After the meal, He Yingqin, accompanied by Liu Duoquan, went to visit at the Friendship Office. At 5:30 PM, he went to the Ning Apartment on Haihe Road in Special District One to rest. He stayed there overnight. Yesterday afternoon at 5:30 PM, He Yingqin met with reporters at the Ning Apartment to discuss his mission in Tianjin, as well as issues such as the Beiping-Shenyang railway opening, the restoration of postal services outside the pass, and the return of the five passes of the Great Wall. The discussion was roughly as follows:

He Yingqin's Remarks

1. I have no particular mission in coming to Tianjin today. I have passed through Tianjin many times before, but have never gotten off the train. Beiping and Tianjin are large cities in the north, and they are very close to each other. Since I came to Beiping, how could I not come to Tianjin? So this time, I specially found an opportunity to come and see. I have some old classmates and prominent figures here whom I haven't seen for a long time, and I want to meet with them today. The return of the five passes of the Great Wall is not a problem. The Japanese side has already agreed on this matter, and it will be implemented as soon as the barracks outside the pass are repaired. It is expected that this can be done soon. Okamura recently went to Beiping, but there was no formal discussion regarding the opening of rail and postal services and the Luandong aftermath. The two sides only exchanged opinions. The opening of rail service may be done in the shortest possible time, but the specific details were not discussed in detail at the recent meeting. I have not heard about the postal service matter. There are also no major difficulties with the Luandong aftermath. The troops stationed in various places will remain the same. As for the conflict between the Tang Yulin and Liu Guitang units in Chahar Province, it was caused by a misunderstanding over disputed territory. Both parties have reported claiming victory, but according to reliable information, the Tang unit may have suffered considerable losses. This matter will be investigated by Commissioner Song Zheyuan nearby, and the true situation will be clarified after the report arrives.

Banquet for Prominent Figures

Last night at 7:00 PM, He Yingqin hosted a banquet for prominent figures from all walks of life at the official residence on Bei Ning Road in Special District One. Those in attendance included Jin Yunpeng, Qi Xieyuan, Sun Chuanfang, Chen Guangyuan, Cao Rulin, Zhang Zitan, Wang Chengbin, Bao Guiqing, Gong Xinzhan, Pan Fu, Gao Lingwei, Cheng Ke, Zhang Zongxiang, Lu Zongyu, Wu Yulin, Zhang Boling, Wang Wenxing, and over fifty others. Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong, Tianjin Mayor Wang Tao, and Yin Tong, Director of the Bei Ning Bureau, also attended as hosts. During the banquet, He Yingqin delivered a speech, saying, "I, Yingqin, was ordered to come to the north, and it has been almost a year now. I have long wanted to find time to come to Tianjin to pay my respects to you gentlemen and receive your teachings, but I have been burdened with military documents and busy affairs. I have been thinking about it for a long time, but it has been difficult to fulfill my wish. Recently, various matters have gradually been sorted out, so I made a special trip here to offer a cup of wine and express my heartfelt admiration and respect. I am honored that you gentlemen have not rejected my humble self and have graced us with your presence for a joyful gathering. You gentlemen have all shouldered significant responsibilities for the country in the past. Although you have now laid down your burdens and are living in seclusion, your responsibility to the country remains the same, whether in or out of office. In my humble opinion, I hope you gentlemen will not hesitate to offer your valuable advice at any time and on any matter. Today, our country is plagued by bandits, year after year of disasters, rural bankruptcy, and industrial and commercial decline. The suffering of the people can be said to be extreme. If we want to alleviate the suffering of the people, we must first eliminate the bandits and revitalize the countryside. We must concentrate the surplus funds from the cities and transfer them to the interior villages as much as possible, and actively engage in construction and revitalization work. We must first ensure that the villagers have food to eat, and then the people in the cities will not starve. On the other hand, we must also find ways to change the psychology of the general public and use the money deposited in large banks in the cities to vigorously develop the border regions, so that the inexhaustible resources can be used to the fullest extent for our benefit. Regarding transportation, the active construction of railways, highways, aviation, and other industries is also a matter of utmost urgency. A week ago, my brothers and I went to inspect the Qinglongqiao area of the Beiping-Suiyuan Railway, and after admiring the bronze statue of Mr. Zhan Tianyou, the creator of the Beiping-Suiyuan Railway, I felt even more that China today needs hundreds of millions of Zhan Tianyous and other talents in order to be saved. If everyone only knows how to set up exchanges and open large stores in a few large cities, exploiting the blood and sweat of the majority for the enjoyment of the minority, then the result of such abnormal development will be of no benefit to the country, and the suffering of the people will only deepen. I also feel that the chaos in the country in recent decades has been due to the decline of national consciousness, and the decline of national consciousness has been due to the degradation of national morality. Because the people of the country regard morality as unimportant, many unfilial, unbrotherly, disloyal, untrustworthy, impolite, unjust, dishonest, and shameless things can be done. The sanctions of the law are not enough to control people's hearts, and the defenses of morality have disappeared. How can the country not be in chaos? How can it not fall into an incurable state? If we want to uplift the sunken hearts and save the declining national situation, the only way is for the government and the people to work together to restore the inherent morality of our nation: filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Only by restoring these inherent virtues can we remedy the shortcomings of the law and enable the Chinese nation to be revived. I also feel that there is still a great crisis lurking in North China today. What is the crisis? It is the secret activities of the Communist Party. The Communist Party was also not noticed in the provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian, but when its power grew, it began to burn, kill, and loot, turning the land red for thousands of miles. Although the activities of the Communist Party in North China are not yet obvious, if we do not think ahead and take precautions, it will become uncontrollable once it breaks out. The method of prevention, if only to hold military police at any time, anywhere detect arrest, prohibit its writing propaganda, at most only stop a while, if to really manage fundamentally, then the first condition, still is to find ways to relieve the people pain, so that the people can live and work in peace, each do their best, to seek the enjoyment of food, clothing, housing and transportation, the second condition, Beijing is to restore national morality, so that everyone takes the eight words of filial piety, brotherly love, loyalty, trustworthiness, propriety, righteousness, integrity and shame as the highest principle of life, then the Communist Party will have no way to take advantage of the opportunity to operate. Some of you gentlemen and I have worked together, and some of you are meeting for the first time. There are many things I want to say, but due to time constraints today, I cannot talk as much as I would like. I am really very sorry. I would like to offer a cup to wish you all good health."

Jin Yunpeng's Reply

After He Yingqin finished his speech, Jin Yunpeng represented the guests in giving a reply, which lasted for an hour and a half. The gist of it was: "It is a great pleasure to hear Mr. He's speech. This is the first time in recent years that we have heard such frank and honest words from the authorities. We are especially grateful for Mr. He's efforts and results in maintaining security in the north. Most of us have held positions of responsibility in governing the country, but we are very ashamed that we have accomplished nothing over the years. We only hope that the current officials will follow Mr. He's words and work in a down-to-earth manner. We must know that although the Chinese nation is now on the verge of collapse, according to historical records, we can assert that there will still be a day of revival. Back when the Five Barbarians caused chaos in China, our Han people were not destroyed. At that time, the Han people in Shandong, Henan, and Hebei were almost completely slaughtered. The situation was even more tragic than the current invasion by the violent Japanese. However, when Emperor Taizong of Tang emerged, the foreign invaders were still swept away, and China was still the world of the Han people. The same is true of the Liao, Jin, Yuan, and Qing dynasties. The reason for this can be deeply considered. It is true that China has thousands of years of culture, a vast territory with abundant resources, and a coastline of over 10,000 li. It is located in the frigid, temperate, and tropical zones, and can be called a land of natural wealth. It has a population of over 500 million, who are able to endure hardship and work hard. With such favorable natural conditions and the addition of human effort, decades or centuries later, we will definitely still be the leaders of the world. Based on this inference, I hope that the people of the country will not be pessimistic. As long as we are realistic and pragmatic, China will not find it difficult to have a day of restoration. Today, all of you gentlemen present, those who were in the government in the past but are now out of office, naturally do not want to change their nationality in middle age and willingly become slaves to a conquered nation. Of course, we will all work together to assist the authorities in overcoming the national crisis. As for communism, I have studied it extensively and firmly believe that it is a doctrine that will destroy our national culture. We absolutely cannot allow it to exist in China. It can be said that it is fortunate for the future of the country that the authorities have made a firm decision on this." (14th)

Active Progress on Opening Railway and Establishing Customs Posts, Iron and Finance Ministries Both Send Specialists North to Assist, Joint Railway Operations Adopted and Railway Bureau's Preparations Ready, Investigation into Establishing Customs at the Six Great Wall Passes Underway

Beiping Correspondence: After Okamura arrived in Beiping and consulted with Huang Fu on various issues between China and Japan in North China, the principles were already determined. Among them, the acceptance of the various passes of the Great Wall was a point of agreement between both parties, and there were no problems. Issues relating to the opening of rail service, establishing customs posts, and restoring postal services, on the other hand, involved the puppet organizations and caused significant disagreements. Official circles have recently determined the necessity of opening the railway and establishing customs as matters of expediency. Regarding the question of the railway, the railway bureau had already proposed plans, which were sent to the Ministry for deliberation and action. The Ministry of Railways also sent specialists, like Guang Yu, north to help. They proposed using the joint operations method. The railway bureau has prepared various procedures and is generally ready to implement them. Everything will be actualized upon the approval of the Ministry. As for the matter of establishing customs, the government's execution is also progressing actively. The Ministry of Finance sent Hanwen, the secretary of the chief tax inspectorate of customs, as a tax inspector, Ding Guitang, to Beiping for contact with the various factions. He was also at the disposal of North China's governing authorities. More recently, Zhang Yongnian, the assistant tax inspector, was sent north to investigate actual circumstances along the Great Wall passes. China's customs regime, as a system, is uniquely special. Even after the September 18th Incident and the loss of the Three Northeast Provinces to the enemy, the customs offices of the northeast were able to carry out their duty until September 15th of last year, when the Japanese formally recognized the puppet state's armed and illegal seizure of customs. China was left with no choice but to formally announce the recall of customs workers on September 25th. It also declared the closure of the customs at Andong, Binkou, Niuzhuang, and Huichun. All the taxes collected were to be replaced by collection at the coast from Jin, Donghai, Jiao, Jianghai, Zhejiang, Min, and Yue sea customs. The customs at Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao have not been occupied to this day. However, Japanese cargo passes through it by relying on its special escorts, without taxation, going over the border, and the tax customs cannot control it. Since the loss of Rehe, to evade customs tax, foreign cargo has taken Rehe as a detour to enter North China, and our customs revenue has decreased, so that there is no way to prevent the dumping of foreign goods. At the same time, the puppet regime established a general customs at Chengde of Rehe, and established branch customs at Luanping, Lingyuan, Chifeng, Pingquan, Gubeikou, and elsewhere. China's cargo bound for the northeast is taxed again and again. Under such circumstances, not only are there massive loopholes, but the impact on national welfare and people's livelihood is extremely significant. This is the reason why the government is planning to establish tax customs at the Great Wall passes. The proposed methods are roughly as follows: A. The nominal question, to avoid involvement of the puppet regime, two methods are planned. (1) The Northeast customs will establish Great Wall posts to perform their duties. (2) To be named the branch posts of the nearby customs. For example, those close to Tianjin, would be named as the branch customs of Jin sea customs, those close to Qinhuangdao, would be named the branch customs of Qinhuangdao, etc. B. The sites of the posts have not been fully determined. After the on-site investigation and observation of the needs, a determination will be made. Those under consideration, in addition to Shanhaiguan, are about Gubeikou, Xifengkou, Panjiakou, Yiyuankou, Jielingkou, Lengkou, and other five locations. C. Methods of taxation, several principles have been decided. (1) Although the northeast has been occupied, it is still our territory. The native goods of the northeast entering the pass are not subject to import tax, but rather a transit tax. (2) The originally designated thirty-six kinds of northeast native goods will continue to be taxed according to the law. Goods other than foreign goods and the thirty-six kinds of native goods that are produced in both the northeast and Japan and Korea will be subject to import tax, in order to prevent the intrusion of foreign goods. (3) Goods transported from the interior to the northeast will not be subject to export tax. (4) Tax rates will remain the same, with no special regulations. Zhang Yongnian, the assistant tax inspector in charge of investigating the actual situation of the Great Wall passes, was originally scheduled to depart yesterday (13th). Appropriately, because of rain and snow, he could not begin the journey. He is now scheduled to travel to the Gubei area with Huo Shi, the director of the Jizhou-Miyun administrative officer's office, to inspect the area. Among the problems of customs tax posts in preparation in the north are, (1) Before full acceptance of the Great Wall passes and complete withdrawal of Japanese soldiers, the realization of the customs posts will be obstructed. (2) Even with the establishment of tax customs posts at each pass, the Japanese side will still have goods transported, as in the story of Shanhaiguan. Under the power of certain strong escorts, they will force passage, and the tax customs will still not be able to control it, then the tax customs at each pass are equal to fictitious posts. The government is paying close attention to this matter. In the sound of our planning and establishment of customs posts, the puppet regime's activity has also been expanding. Yesterday, Gao Yanagi Shigejiro, the Japanese supervisor director of the puppet Chengde tax customs, arrived at Qian'an with more than twenty personnel, claiming that the puppet regime planned to establish a tax customs along the border between Qian'an and Rehe, to collect customs tax, and has come to investigate. (November 14th)

It has been decided to order the two brigades of Zhang Luanji and Liu Shangzhi to advance towards Chong'an, and the two brigades of Zhou Zhiqun and Situ Fei to advance towards Guangze, in coordination with the Guomindang armies of Jiangxi and Zhejiang. As for the rehabilitation of the bandit area, it has been decided to form a Rehabilitation Committee for Northern Fujian, to be established by the end of this month. Work will begin next month, and efforts will be made to gather the refugees back to their hometowns and restore rural order within a short period of time. In addition, the newly appointed Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Dai Ji, arrived in Xiamen a few days ago and was invited by Mao Weishou, Commander of the 61st Division, to visit Quanzhou yesterday. Chiang Kai-shek Cables Wang Jingwei and Kong Xiangxi, Requesting Prompt Allocation of Short-Term Relief Funds, To Allocate 2 Million Yuan in Full Within Three Months, To Handle Rehabilitation in Bandit Areas, So That It Can Advance in Parallel with Military Operations

Nanchang Correspondence: Chiang Kai-shek recently submitted a proposal through the Central Political Council to allocate 15 million yuan for long-term rehabilitation and 2 million yuan for short-term relief to bandit-affected areas, and also formulated various methods for long-term and short-term relief. However, the short-term relief funds have not yet been allocated by the central government, causing considerable difficulties in preparing for rehabilitation. He recently telegraphed President Wang Jingwei and Minister Kong Xiangxi again, requesting that the 2 million yuan for short-term relief be allocated in full within three months as soon as possible, so that military operations would not be hindered by politics and could advance in parallel. It is said that Wang and Kong have replied by telegram that they will do their best to raise funds to meet the urgent needs. The following is Chiang's telegram to Wang and Kong: "Respectfully acknowledge the Fish Secret Telegram. The 1.8 million yuan for short-term relief for bandit-affected areas is purely for the needs of accommodating refugees, distributing emergency relief, relocating the elderly, weak, and disabled, reforming and educating those who have surrendered, organizing local militias, establishing blockades, constructing bunkers, building roads, and appropriately calculating construction costs, as well as subsidizing all county and district administration expenses in recovered areas. It must be complementary to the progress of military operations; otherwise, even if military operations are successful, they will be completely ineffective. The various bandit forces in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui have been successively defeated, and the campaign in the central and northwestern parts of Jiangxi is also nearing completion. However, the necessary emergency facilities following the army cannot advance in parallel due to a lack of funds, causing military operations to be delayed and unable to develop rapidly. The importance of this relationship has been described in detail in the telegrams of August (August) and May (21). In the Dongwei telegram of this month, it was repeatedly stated that all of the above uses are all urgent needs that cannot be delayed at present. Since the Political Conference approved the order on August 25th, the Ministry of Finance has been ordered to allocate the funds in full. However, several months have passed, and no amount has been actually provided. The headquarters has been transferring funds from the east to the west to cope with the situation, and it has now reached a point where it cannot continue to do so. Brother Yongzhi has only agreed to borrow 200,000 yuan in advance, which is not only a drop in the bucket but also of no use. Moreover, the work of military advancement and short-term rehabilitation cannot be interrupted. No matter how difficult it may be, please make every effort to raise the 1.8 million yuan for short-term relief within three months and allocate it in installments. (Omission) I eagerly await a satisfactory reply." (November 14th)

<Budget Preparation Procedures P]

(1) From the year 1935, all Boxer Indemnity funded institutions must, before January 15th of each year, prepare their respective institutional budgets for the following year, along with a statement of intended uses, and submit them to the Executive Yuan for review by the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics and the Ministry of Education. (2) For the year 1934, the budgets and statements of intended uses should be submitted to the Executive Yuan two months before the original time of budget preparation by the institutions. (2) The aforementioned reviewing bodies should, within one month, submit their review opinions to the Executive Yuan for transmittal to the respective Boxer Indemnity funded institutions, so that they may take note during budget preparation. (3) After the aforementioned budgets and statements have been prepared, the respective Boxer Indemnity funded institutions should immediately submit them to the Executive Yuan's Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Finance, and the National Audit Office for record keeping.

Accounting and Verification Issues (1) After the end of each fiscal year, all Boxer Indemnity funded institutions must promptly submit their respective institutional final accounts and monthly income and expenditure reports to the Executive Yuan for transmission to the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics and the National Audit Office for verification. (2) The Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics and the National Audit Office should, within three months, submit their verification opinions to the Executive Yuan for transmittal to the various institutions for attention, and also inform the Ministry of Education.

Institutional Cooperation Issues (1) To promote centralized cooperation and increase efficiency in the educational and cultural endeavors of the various Boxer Indemnity funded institutions, the Executive Yuan should establish an inter-institutional joint meeting for Boxer Indemnity affairs. (2) Starting in 1935, the aforementioned joint meeting shall be convened by the Executive Yuan on the twelfth of each month for a regular meeting to discuss the important principles regarding the use of funds for educational and cultural endeavors in the budgets of the various Boxer Indemnity funded institutions for the following year, or other important matters. (In 1934, meetings shall be held once each in March and December.) (3) The aforementioned meeting shall be organized by the following personnel: Each Boxer Indemnity funded institution, or its Chinese delegation, shall nominate one or two representatives; the Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, the Director of Political Affairs, the Minister of Education, and the Vice Minister. The Premier of the Executive Yuan shall chair the meeting. (4) Before the meeting, each Boxer Indemnity funded institution, or its Chinese delegation, must submit to the Executive Yuan in writing the amount of funds and plans regarding the use of funds for educational and cultural endeavors in the institution's budget for the following year. (5) The results of the discussions at the aforementioned meeting, after being decided by the Executive Yuan and notified to the various Boxer Indemnity funded institutions, or their Chinese delegations, should be vigorously promoted for implementation. (6) The aforementioned joint meeting should have one secretary, who shall, under the orders of the Premier of the Executive Yuan, manage all affairs related to the meeting during the period of the meeting and before and after the meeting. (The Premier shall appoint or select a dedicated person from among the Executive Yuan staff to serve in this role.)

Guangdong Provincial Army to Be Reorganized

Xiang Hanping and Li Yangjing Resign Successively

Miao Peinan Appointed Deputy Commander of the Second Army

Huang Renhuan Succeeds as Commander of the Third Army

Each Army Increases Strength by One Division into a Three-Division System

Guangzhou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has recently been quite active in reorganizing military affairs. Xiang Hanping, Commander of the Second Army, has submitted his resignation, which has been approved by Chen Jitang, who will concurrently serve as Commander of the Second Army. It is reported that Mr. Xiang left Guangzhou on the evening of handing over military authority. Chen Jitang, in order to reorganize the future army units, convened a military conference once on the morning of the 10th at 9:00 AM. Li Yangjing, Commander of the Third Army, was not present and submitted his resignation. Those who attended on that day included Yu Hanmou, Miao Peinan, Du Yiqian, Wu Fan, Zhang Zhiying, Tang Haoqing, etc. During the meeting, the reorganization of the military system was proposed and discussed in great detail. Some suggested abolishing the army commander and taking the division as the unit. Others suggested maintaining the current military system and expanding it to a three-division structure for each army. The majority favored the latter proposal. However, since each army currently only has two divisions, it is necessary to add one division to complete the three-division quota. The method is to merge the independent divisions into the various armies, i.e., the Independent Third Division under Li Hanhun will be reorganized into the Third Division of the First Army, the Teaching Division under Miao Peinan will be reorganized into the Sixth Division of the Second Army, and the Independent First Division under Huang Renhuan will be reorganized into the Ninth Division of the Third Army. The Independent Fourth Division will be renamed the Independent First Division. The detailed measures will be handed over to the Military Affairs Department to formulate the establishment, and then formally announced. The establishment of each army has been roughly drafted, but the selection of senior military officers for the assignment was also discussed during the meeting. As a result, Miao Peinan, Commander of the Rescue Teaching Division, will be promoted to Deputy Commander of the Second Army, Zhang Guoyuan will be transferred to Chief of Staff of the Second Army, Tan Sui, Deputy Commander of the Teaching Division, will be promoted to Commander of the Teaching Division, and Huang Renhuan, Commander of the Independent First Division, will succeed Li Yangjing, who has earnestly resigned, as Commander of the Third Army. Zhou Zhi, former Chief of Staff of the Third Army, will be transferred to Major General Staff Officer of the First Army Group Headquarters. Deng Qing'ao, Director of the Military Supply Department and Director of the Rear Affairs Office of the Third Army, has also been dismissed. The vacancy will be filled by Jian Zuozhen, the current Counselor of the Headquarters. After the military conference on the 10th, the society still feels calm as usual. If there are no other problems, it will be implemented in accordance with the resolution. Regarding the air force, there have also been some new arrangements in recent days. Yesterday, the Air Force Department transferred the Third Air Squadron stationed in Shaozhou, Beijiang back to the province, and transferred the Sixth Squadron under Ma Tinghuai to Shaozhou for defense. The Fifth Air Squadron under Wu Jianwen recently destroyed two aircraft in Meixian, and four airmen were killed. It is now planned to send several more aircraft to replenish them. (November 14th)

Songjiang

Petty Thief Commits Murder of Victim

A resident with the surname of a certain village in the ninth district of Punan Ninglong Temple, who was of modest wealth, had been coveted by thieves. It was heard that around midnight on the 15th, the whole family was asleep when thieves pried open the front door, intending to commit theft. The victim heard the sound of something being pried open and knew what was happening, so he got up to investigate. He spotted a thief on the ladder, groping around in the dark. The victim remained quiet and approached to capture him, but the thief suddenly became aware and took out the sharp knife he was carrying to resist. The victim was caught off guard and was stabbed in a vital spot, falling to the ground and crying out in pain. The family was alarmed and got up to see what was happening. The murderer immediately fled through the door, and the victim died from his serious injuries shortly thereafter. The village police from that district have rushed to Songjiang to report to the County Court and request an investigation. It is reported that the Procuratorate will send personnel to the village on the 17th for an on-site investigation.

Zhenjiang

Construction of Eight Township Pond Projects

The Zhenjiang County Pond Project Committee, in order to alleviate the rural economy, raised funds to build pond and water conservancy projects in various townships, which has been going on for three or four years. The third phase of the project this year started in ten townships, with a total of 797 ponds dredged. In addition, Huangxu New Village undertook the construction of several ponds and dams. The San Yi River in Jinshan was dredged for 80 feet, and the excavated soil was estimated to be about 50,000 to 60,000 portions, benefiting many fields. Today, the Committee convened the fourth phase of the project meeting, chaired by Committee Member Liu. More than a dozen surveyors and assistants from various townships attended the meeting. The matters resolved were: (1) Starting from the 11th of this month, the pond projects in Dantu, Renrang, Changle, Gaozi, Shangdang, Suifeng, Yucheng, and Chongde eight townships will be launched. (2) The construction of the embankment in Yonggu Township will be handled by Committee Member Xu. The pond and dam project in Xinfeng Township will be handled by Huangxu New Village, which is run by Committee Member. Whether the Jianbi Township can be handled will be decided within two months. (3) The townships to be investigated in this phase are Changle, Gaozi, Shangdang, and Suifeng four townships, and the fourth district of Renrang should also be investigated. (4) This phase promotes the construction of sluice gates and dams in various townships, starting with Shangdang, Suifeng, Changle, Yucheng, Dantu, and Gaozi six townships. A dam protection agreement will be formulated separately to allow farmers to take turns managing them.

Hangzhou

Female Student Falsely Accused of Obtaining Money, Detained in Court

Zhang Helian, a Hangzhou native who once studied at the Hangzhou Women's Vocational School, is now over 20 years old and is dressed fashionably. She lives at No. 155 Qingtai Road, which was moved to Pingpingfang, Huixing Road this spring. She has a female friend named Zhang Zijie who is in financial difficulties. Zijie borrowed 15 yuan from Zhang. The day before yesterday, Zhang went to collect the debt. Zijie was unable to repay it. Helian said that she had an urgent need and now had no money. She had a local bank's 1,000 yuan fixed deposit passbook and asked her to help introduce her to pledge 400 yuan to meet the urgent need. Zijie agreed and helped to introduce the mortgage. Helian immediately took out a passbook and handed it to Zijie. After Zijie got the passbook, she secretly ordered her sister to inquire. The local bank informed her that one yuan in the passbook had been altered to one thousand yuan and wanted to detain her and send her to the Public Security Bureau for handling. After repeated discussions, and claiming that Zhang Helian would be arrested, she was allowed to return home and informed her sister, who reported to the police station to arrest Zhang and send her to the District Court for handling.

Local News

Kong Xiangxi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday to Discuss the Central Government's Attitude Towards the Fujian Incident

Differing Opinions Should Be Addressed with Frankness

If the Worst Comes to Pass, Political Methods Will Be Used to Resolve the Issue

Greatly Hope that Mr. Hu Hanmin Will Go to Beijing as Soon as Possible

Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi arrived in Shanghai by overnight train at 7:30 yesterday morning. He returned to his private residence on West Avenues Road for rest. Ms. Soong Mei-ling, wife of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who flew to Shanghai from Jiangxi the day before yesterday, visited Mr. Kong around 9:00 yesterday morning and had a conversation for about half an hour. At 11:00, Mr. Kong met with reporters from various newspapers and then went to the Central Bank to work.

The following is a record of Mr. Kong's remarks:

The Change in the Fujian Situation Seems Unbelievable

According to Mr. Kong, there have been widespread rumors in recent days that there will be changes in the Fujian situation. The central government has not yet received accurate reports on this matter. Chairman Lin will arrive in Beijing today (yesterday), and the truth should be revealed. However, according to my observation, at this time of serious national crisis, the people of the whole country are united to seek national salvation. Fujian Province will never take advantage of the opportunity to make changes and promote the reason for destruction. The 19th Route Army has made great contributions to resisting Japan and suppressing bandits and will never destroy its glorious history and make relatives sad and enemies happy. Moreover, the leaders of the Fujian Incident who are rumored outside all have a long history with our party and will never take actions that endanger the party and the country. Even if there are any differences of opinion, it should not be difficult to suggest to the central government without taking any rash actions.

The Central Government's Attitude Is to Meet with Sincerity

When reporters asked what the central government would do if the rumors unfortunately became a reality, Mr. Kong replied that the central government adopted an attitude of meeting with sincerity towards all parties. If unfortunately, the rumors became a reality, the central government would be magnanimous and resolve the issue through political methods. In short, at this time of internal and external troubles, the country is in danger. All Chinese people must unite sincerely and work together to save the situation. The central government is making every effort to unite within the party, and it also sincerely hopes that all parties will unite and concentrate the power of the whole country to strive hard.

Hope Mr. Hu Will Go to Beijing as Soon as Possible

Since the September 18th Incident, the central government has always taken unity against foreign aggression as its main purpose in order to save the country. Therefore, it is hoped that Mr. Hu Zhantang, who is living in Hong Kong, will focus on national affairs and return to Beijing to take office as soon as possible. Mr. Hu previously stayed in Hong Kong for recuperation due to illness. Recently, his health has gradually recovered. The comrades of the central government regard Mr. Hu as one of the standing committee members of the Central Political Council and sincerely hope that he will come to Beijing as soon as possible to share the arduous tasks. Mr. Hu is an advanced member of our party and has a long history with our party and the General. He will never betray our party. Mr. Kong believes that the rumors that Mr. Hu is going to Fujian or even that Mr. Hu has arrived in Fujian are definitely not accurate.

A Financial Conference Is Not Necessary for the Time Being

Mr. Kong also talked about the central government's finances, saying that the central government's finances are based on increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. I have said this repeatedly. For example, in economic principles, Denald (demand) and Supply (supply) must be consistent. Those in charge of finance must also ensure that legitimate needs have legitimate supply, that is, so-called measuring income to determine expenditure and measuring expenditure to determine income. As for convening a national financial conference, there is no need for it at present. We should "do more and meet less."

Post-Disaster Relief in Bandit Areas to Be Remitted for One Month First

Finally, when reporters asked about Chairman Chiang's request for the allocation of funds for post-disaster relief in bandit areas, Mr. Kong said that the work of treating the symptoms in bandit areas should be actively carried out. People who are unwilling to be ravaged by bandits and flee from bandit areas must be given relief. Relief must have expenses. This matter was originally approved by the Central Political Council for 1.8 million yuan. Chairman Chiang had previously telegraphed to request allocation. The funds were agreed to be paid in three months. The Ministry of Finance has first remitted 600,000 yuan for the first month, etc.

Security and Transportation Have Been Agreed Upon

The Two Routes Air Defense Committee invited military and police agencies in Shanghai to discuss the security and transportation of the naming ceremony of the aircraft on the two routes at the Two Routes Administration Bureau conference room yesterday. Li Guangzeng (Public Security Bureau), Wang Enchi (Security Office), Sun Jiaqian (Public Works Bureau), Li (Public Security Bureau), Lin Wojiang, Wu Yucang, Guo Xuezhang (China Aviation Association), Xie, Gong Guodong (Two Routes Police Station), Chen Yixin, Zheng Youshang (Songhu Garrison Headquarters), Li Dasan, Zou Zhengjian, Wei Yunlou, Zhang Yunhe, Xie Chengyu, Yuan Boyang, Chen Chengshi (Two Routes Party Headquarters) Chairman Yuan Boyang (Xie Chengyu acting) attended the meeting. After the chairman reported the significance of the meeting, he said that the naming ceremony of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo aircraft would be held at 2:00 pm on the 18th of this month. Today, we invite everyone to come together to discuss and resolve the security and maintenance of traffic order at the conference. The comrades of the two routes are very grateful for your willingness to come. Then, the following resolutions were discussed and passed: (A) Conference security, (1) The conference venue is divided into two parts for security inside and outside the venue. (2) The security inside the venue is jointly responsible by the Security Office, Garrison Headquarters, and the Two Routes Police Station. (3) The security outside the venue is the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau.
