(5) The train to and from Xujiahui donated by the Two Routes comrades to the "Government 克持士" aircraft station is responsible for maintaining order by six military police officers from the military police company stationed at the North Station. (6) Each truck from Xujiahui to the Hongqiao Airport is maintained by a military police officer from the Garrison Headquarters, a total of fifteen trucks. (7) The order of the Xujiahui Station is maintained by ten police officers from the Public Security Bureau. (8) The commander-in-chief of the military police at the conference is appointed by the Garrison Headquarters. (9) The security inside the venue will be completed before 12:00 noon on the 18th, and the security outside the venue will be completed before 12:00 noon. (B) The conference military band is appointed by the Public Security Bureau. (C) The admission tickets for the conference are checked jointly by the road police boy scouts, the Public Security Bureau, and the conference staff. (D) One-way traffic route, (1) The outbound route goes directly to the airport from Hongqiao Road. (2) The return route returns to Shanghai from Paifang Road, Pears Road, and Yuyuan Road. (E) The admission certificates for news reporters and photographers are distributed by the Shanghai China Aviation Association.

Sun Tonggang's Ambition

To Fly to Southeast Asia and the World

Sponsored by the Flying Society But Did Not Donate Aircraft

Aviator Tonggang came to Shanghai this time to accept the aircraft donated by Mr. Du Yuesheng. He test-flew at the Hongqiao Airport the day before yesterday with excellent results. Yesterday, Mr. Sun told reporters that he planned to stay in Shanghai for another four or five days and then take the aircraft donated by Mr. Du back to Jinan. Sun also said that this time he returned to China with four major goals. First, to complete the Euro-Asia cross-country flight, which has been fulfilled as desired. Second, to fly across the country, which has also been successful recently. Third, to fly to Southeast Asia, which is planned to pass through Hong Kong, Guangzhou, Manila, Singapore, Sumatra, Java, Sanbaolong, and other places back to China. However, this flight has more sea routes than land routes, which is different from the previous Euro-Asia cross-country flight, which had more land routes than sea routes. Therefore, it is necessary to purchase a new type of aircraft that can be used for long-distance flights. For this reason, it can be realized at the end of this year or in the spring of next year. After the third goal is completed, he will go to Germany again to carefully study aircraft manufacturing, hoping to gain something. Finally, he prepares to complete the fourth goal, which is to fly around the world. At that time, he may compete with aviators from all over the world and win glory for the motherland. Mr. Sun finally said that he extremely approved of the Flying Society and hoped that it would achieve something as soon as possible. However, Mr. Lin Wojiang said yesterday that he would donate the new aircraft donated to him by Mr. Du Yuesheng to the Flying Society, which was not true. However, he would assist in the progress of the Society as much as possible.

Hu Hanmin Still Residing in Hong Kong

Chen Jitang Urges Hu to Enter Beijing

Changes in the Fujian Situation Difficult to Realize

According to the Central News Agency, rumors have been circulating for days that there will be changes in the political situation in Fujian Province, and that Mr. Hu Zhantang, a member of the Central Committee, has arrived in Fujian, etc. Yesterday, the reporter specifically visited a friend of Mr. Hu to inquire about Mr. Hu's whereabouts. Moreover, as far as I know, Chen Bonan (Jitang) also urged Mr. Hu to enter Beijing as soon as possible to realize sincere unity. The planning of the Fujian Incident was only the trivial act of politicians close to Chen Zhenru (Mingshu) and some intellectuals from the so-called Third Party and Social Democratic Party. Gui Army generals Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, etc., do not approve of it. The so-called five provinces in the Southwest are even castles in the air. Therefore, changes in the Fujian situation are difficult to realize.

He hopes to go south to Beijing within a few days to meet Chairman Lin. Poskery will also go to Ping to meet Marconi. Three Parties to Negotiate the Construction of a Large Freight Depot at the North Station

Grain Industry Suggests

Postal Savings Bureau Invests

Road Bureau Leases

Shanghai Times News from This Port: The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways Administration, in order to develop its business, greatly reduced the rent for the two railways' freight depots, changing the daily rent from five cents to one cent and five mills per ton. This was announced and implemented in June of this year. However, in recent months, business in Shanghai has declined, and grains stored in the warehouses have piled up like mountains and cannot be circulated. The Traffic Department had no choice but to notify the Grain Industry Association to restore the old price, hoping that customers would submit their goods as soon as possible. However, the Grain Industry Association, in this economic downturn, suddenly increased its burden by more than three times. It wrote to the two railways to express its opposition and sent Chairman Gu to negotiate in person. Now, Railway Director Huang Boqiao has agreed with Post Office Savings and Remittance Bureau Director Tang Baoshu to invest in the two railways to build a freight depot near the North Station as a fundamental solution. The details are recorded below:

Grain Industry Association's Reply Letter

Gu Xinyi, Chairman of the Grain Industry Association, sent a letter to the two railways yesterday, which read, "Respectfully, on November 4th, a letter was approved by the Traffic Department stating that the warehouses at the Maigen Road freight station of this railway were full of goods and could not be discharged. Now it is autumn, new goods are on the market, and foreign stations are continuously transporting them, but there is no warehouse space to stack them. Now, in order to clear the goods, the free storage period for goods at the station will be temporarily changed to five days from the 3rd of this month. In addition, the storage fee for all fourth-class and below goods will be temporarily charged according to the third-class goods storage rate, that is, zero-load will be calculated and charged per 50 kilograms (or less), and the whole car will be calculated and charged per ton (or less). We hereby inform you that we hope you will check and inform your colleagues, etc. With this, the loading and unloading of goods has been greatly facilitated. Therefore, the railway bureau's income has also increased sharply at the same time. This is a win-win situation. However, after only four months, the Traffic Department suddenly changed it again. Then, the original intention of the revision of the price at that time should be considered a temporary strategy to attract freight. In order to clear the accumulated goods, it is like abandoning food because of choking. Moreover, at this time when farmers and merchants are in trouble and the whole country is seeking to revitalize the countryside, reducing freight is regarded as an important plan. The Traffic Department has instead created this price increase for grains due to the full load of freight. No matter whether it is temporary or long-term, it should not be taken by your bureau. Therefore, we hereby inform you that we respectfully ask you to consider it and transfer it to the Traffic Department to develop other methods to clear the accumulated goods. The original situation should be maintained for grain transportation. We respectfully request a reply, etc. Sincerely, Gu Xin, Chairman of the Grain Industry Association, etc.

Adding Freight Depots to the North Station

During this period when the central government is seeking to clear the national grain and the Eight Provinces Grain Conference has also resolved to reduce freight rates, the authorities of the two railways suddenly took the initiative to increase the warehouse rent for grain, which is not a fundamental solution. After Gu Xinyi and others tried their best to negotiate, the railway bureau also believed that the fundamental solution was to add freight depots to seek clearance. However, it is not easy to raise funds for adding huge freight depots. The director of the two railways has discussed the results with Director Tang Baoshu of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, and it has been decided that the Savings and Remittance Bureau will invest in the two railways to build freight depots. Yesterday afternoon, Mo Heng, a representative of the two railways, and Xu Yuanfang, a representative of the Savings and Remittance Bureau, went to the Grain Industry Association with Gu Xinyi to discuss together and decided: (1) The two railways will relocate to a suitable location at the North Station for the construction of a huge freight depot. (2) The construction cost of the freight depot will be invested by the Savings and Remittance Bureau. (3) The freight depot must be able to accommodate at least 5,000 tons of goods. (4) Before the freight depot is built, a temporary freight depot capable of accommodating 5,000 tons will be built first. (5) After the temporary freight depot is successfully built, the previous warehouse rent will be restored. (6) After the Savings and Remittance Bureau has successfully built the depot, the Railway Bureau will rent it for use. If there are no goods to stack in the future, the Grain Industry Association will rent it as much as possible on its behalf to avoid losses, etc.

Chiang Orders Six Provinces to Strictly Urge Powerful and Wealthy Families to Pay Overdue Taxes 丨丨 Follows Orders to Review and Reduce Surcharges 丨丨

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, considering that the surcharges on land taxes in various provinces are excessively high, exceeding the regular tax by several times, while the regular tax itself is decreasing daily, attributes the cause to powerful gentry and wealthy families defaulting on taxes as if they were exempt, while the weak and small people alone bear the heavy burden. This is a common problem in all provinces. In addition to having previously telegraphed eight provinces to earnestly review and reduce land tax surcharges, he has now telegraphed the chairmen and finance directors of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Henan provinces to earnestly review and reduce land tax surcharges to alleviate the people's hardships. At the same time, he orders strict collection of overdue taxes from powerful and wealthy families to eliminate long-standing malpractices and increase tax revenue. The original telegram stated: "It has been found that in recent years, the surcharges on land taxes in various provinces have been excessively high, often exceeding the regular tax by several times, while at the same time, the fixed amount of land tax collected has been decreasing daily. The reason for this is that powerful gentry and wealthy families in various localities, landlords who own a large amount of land, mostly rely on their power to delay payment. Tax collectors dare not do anything about it, and local officials are also often afraid and accommodating. This has become a long-standing habit, virtually equivalent to exemption. Even their clansmen and relatives rely on their protection and take advantage of their power to resist tax collection, resulting in ever-increasing arrears and a great impact on tax revenue. Therefore, both the regular tax and surcharges are borne solely by the weak and small people who own little land, while the powerful and cunning do not participate. This phenomenon has become a common problem in almost all provinces, which is not only the source of local financial difficulties but also the main cause of rural bankruptcy and the people's distress. The provincial governments should immediately rectify and thoroughly reform this situation. On the one hand, the land tax surcharges should be earnestly reviewed and reduced in accordance with the telegram of □ day, without exceeding the ratio set by the Ministry of Finance, to alleviate the people's hardships. On the other hand, the amount and names of those in arrears for past years should be investigated, a deadline should be set, and strict collection should be enforced, without allowing arrears to accumulate. If there are still those who rely on their power to resist payment, public officials currently serving in the Party, government, or military should have their positions and titles in the central or local organs investigated, and a request should be made to dismiss them and order them to return the funds. If they are local gentry, they should be immediately arrested and severely punished. If their relatives and family members delay or resist payment, the relevant officials and gentry will be held accountable, and those who shield them will be punished for the same crime. If they fail to pay by the deadline, their property will be investigated and confiscated separately, or their land on which taxes are not paid will be confiscated to compensate. It is hoped that this will be strictly implemented with great efficiency. After the order is issued, if the county magistrate fears difficulties and acts leniently, failing to make effective efforts in collection, or if the provincial departments perfunctorily delay and do not take charge, they should be strictly investigated according to the circumstances, and their crimes should be discussed and judged separately. It is hoped that everyone will strictly abide by this and instruct their subordinates to comply as well." (November 14th)

Inspection Report on Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei Provinces By Our Special Correspondent, Ren An The Current Situation on the Xiangyang-Hankou Road and in Zaoyang

Zaoyang Correspondence: Returning to Hankou from an inspection of eastern Hubei, I then made a trip to northern Hubei, taking the Pinghan Railway. Because I wanted to catch the Xiang(yang)-Hua(yuan) bus the next morning, I took the ordinary express train at 7:00 PM, from Han(kou) to Hua(yuan). The train was delayed by loading goods along the way, and only arrived at midnight. Although I could not see the scenery outside the window along the way, I did witness several scenes of tragedy, which are worth recounting.

The vehicles used this time were mostly old and dilapidated, and there were no doors connecting the cars. When checking tickets, the ticket inspector had to go up and down through the middle doors on both sides. Perhaps there were not enough personnel assigned. In the car I was in, there were only three ticket inspectors. Among the passengers, there was an old man from Henan who had failed to find work in Hankou and was returning to his hometown with his family. He was found to have no ticket and only produced two yuan and several jiao in coins, saying as he turned his pockets inside out, "I don't have a single copper coin left." The ticket inspector searched his body, and then his family. Suddenly, from a cigarette case, he poured out two or three yuan in banknotes. The ticket inspector quickly shone a flashlight on the ground, picked up the money, and hid it in his trouser pocket. The old man demanded it back but was unsuccessful and spoke inappropriately, and was slapped in the face by the ticket inspector, who said, "You said you didn't have a single copper coin, where did these banknotes come from?" Having said that, he did not issue a temporary ticket and turned away. In the next seat, I happened to meet a soldier with untidy clothes, who was asked to pay for a half-price ticket. The soldier seemed to have something to rely on and roared loudly, "If everyone here can get a half-price ticket, I will follow suit. Otherwise, I am not that old man, don't even think about bullying me again." Later, the ticket inspector ordered him to produce his passport, or he would be ordered off the train immediately. The soldier became enraged and punched the ticket inspector in the face, hitting him in the chest, and said, "Dare you look at my passport?" At that moment, the train arrived at Xiaogan, and they wrestled each other off the train. Then the passengers in the car began to discuss the matter loudly. A cotton merchant named Mr. Kong, who often traveled this route, claimed that the regulations on the Pinghan Railway were quite strict at first, but over time, they became lax and opened up loopholes. Once, when he was traveling south on this route, he saw several soldiers walking back and forth in the car, whispering to passengers. Later, they brought several sets of military uniforms and put them on the passengers, and even mixed one or two people without military uniforms among them. When the ticket inspector arrived, the soldier would simply say, "These passengers are under my care," or "Newly recruited soldiers." The ticket inspector would then nod silently and leave. However, the passengers who temporarily wore military uniforms or mixed in with military uniforms still had to secretly prepare half the ticket price to give to the soldier who was taking care of them and the ticket inspector who nodded silently. "They work together to share the spoils, deceiving only the public," he said. Another passenger whispered, "Half-price tickets for soldiers are a thing of the past. Now, not only do few people buy half-price tickets, but they even use military purposes as an excuse to transport retail goods. In terms of ticket inspection, there are also cases of issuing temporary tickets but forgetting to tear off the ticket stubs," and so on. Before long, a snoring adjutant suddenly announced that he had lost a hundred yuan in banknotes, and pointed to a soldier who he knew had the money as the biggest suspect. However, the soldier was sitting far away in another corner, and the two sides argued, almost leading to the final act. When the train arrived at the Huayuan station, it was a pity that I had to get off the train and did not get to see the whole picture.

The next morning, at 4:30 AM, I went from the train station to the bus station, passing through Hezhou, which was two or three li wide. The travelers walked in single file, groping forward in the dark night on the sandy beach, unable to distinguish the path, and following the porters. However, as the east gradually turned white, the sky gradually became brighter, and the morning exercises and bugle calls of the troops encamped on both banks were carried by the wind. When I arrived at the station, I saw several bungalows and inns, with recruiting flags slantedly inserted. Because the bus was used to transport both people and goods, the ride was particularly uncomfortable. Moreover, to guard against bandits, several buses traveled in convoy, stirring up dust and making breathing difficult. Passing through Luan and arriving at Suixian (that is, the State of Sui in the Spring and Autumn Period), a journey of two hundred and some li, the bus stopped to change goods. I took a trip to the city. The city has two layers of walls, an inner stone wall and an outer earth wall. The garrison troops are very strong. The city is home to the headquarters of the 34th Brigade, led by Brigadier Luo, who is known for his strict military orders, especially against opium smokers. Regardless of whether they are soldiers or civilians, they are killed if caught. Jiyang is about two hundred li away from here and is still within the brigade's defense area. However, a certain deputy brigade commander does not supervise the troops very strictly, and the discipline of the stationed troops is far inferior to this. There are about one hundred and some bandits in Suixian, who appear and disappear in the mountains and do not cause much harm. However, due to the terrain, there is a risk of robbery on the traffic between Sui and Zao. Recently, there have been two robberies of buses. The bandits, only three or five people, first fired shots to stop the bus, then overturned the boxes and baskets, and drove the passengers off the bus, strictly ordering them to hand over any hidden money, otherwise they would be shot if caught. Some passengers who had money left over, in order to save their lives, took it out from their collars, boots, and hats, and respectfully presented it to the bandits. Later, they drove the bus to a designated wilderness area. Only then did I return and sit on the roadside waiting for the passengers. On another occasion, the bandits disguised themselves as merchants, hid weapons, and when they reached a certain location, they threatened to stop the bus and did whatever they wanted. The bandits are mostly natives, making it difficult to detect them. The robberies have not killed or stripped people of their clothes. Stripping people of their clothes in the winter would freeze them to death, which is still a sign of some conscience not being completely extinguished. When the rear bus continued west to Zaoyang from Suixian, it was seen that escort teams had been added. White flags waved in the wind, tightly following each passenger and cargo bus. Moreover, when the bus started, the passengers were searched with extreme thoroughness, especially to prevent the carrying of weapons. As for whether they had passports or local goods, it seemed that no one cared. All the way, we passed through mountain slopes and highlands, which had been plagued by banditry and drought for years. The fields were desolate, and the dilapidated villages rarely showed signs of life. The residents were starving and cold, and many of them resorted to desperate measures. The endless cycle of banditry is probably not without reason.

Two years ago, Zaoyang County, outside the city walls, had almost completely fallen into the hands of the Red Army. Later, due to the efforts of the Independent 34th Brigade in stationing and suppressing the bandits, the people in the rear provided supplies, and the soldiers were encouraged to fight bravely, the bandit areas were gradually recovered. However, because the area is adjacent to southern Henan, large groups of Henan bandits often come to the border to harass the area. Moreover, because of the two disasters of banditry and drought, bad causes have been created, so sporadic small bandits and robberies on the main roads still occur from time to time. Moreover, these local bandits are more difficult to defend against than the large Henan bandits, because they are natives and like attached bones, coming out at night and hiding during the day, making suppression and pacification very difficult. Recently, when cotton was put on the market, many cotton merchants passing through the nearby city walls were robbed. The county government has offered a reward to encourage people to capture and kill them. The reward is 400 yuan for capturing them alive on the spot, 200 yuan for reporting and arresting them, and 100 yuan for killing them and providing proof. The opium scourge in northern Hubei has recently spread again. The county has an opium rehabilitation center, and the districts have opium rehabilitation sub-centers. Opium addicts pay a rehabilitation fee of one yuan per month, and the number of addicts is only allowed to decrease, not increase. In practice, the result is the opposite. Sellers pay a special tax, the amount of which is based on the prosperity of their business, generally ranging from dozens to hundreds of yuan per month. Other peculiar customs will be described later.

The Gengkuan (Boxer Indemnity) Funds Organizations Decide on Various Matters Recently Convened by the Executive Yuan All Matters Have Been Submitted to the National Government for Record

The Executive Yuan convened a meeting of various Gengkuan funds organizations on the 6th of this month, and resolved three issues regarding the budget formulation process, two issues regarding reimbursement and review, and six issues regarding cooperation among Gengkuan funds organizations. A report was submitted to the Yuan meeting on the 14th and was approved, and reported to the National Government for record. A letter was sent to the Secretariat of the Political Council for forwarding, and separate orders were sent to the relevant agencies to implement them. The original text is recorded as follows:

The West District Property Appraisal Table Has Been Printed

The property appraisal table for the West District of the Public Concession has been printed and contains the registered numbers, land numbers, and assessed values of the properties in the district, as well as an attached map. Those wishing to purchase it may contact the Donation Collection Office of the Public Concession at 209 Jiangxi Road.

Sanitary Conditions in the International Settlement

The acting director of the Health Department of the Public Concession reported in October that the general public health was the same as in September. There were no special issues to note, except for the death of a child in a family due to smallpox after refusing vaccination. There has been a significant increase in cases of diphtheria in children, and parents and school authorities should pay attention. Scarlet fever should also not be ignored. In general, attention should be paid to sore throats during this season.

Mortality Statistics: The mortality rate for foreigners this month was 8.42 per thousand, and for Chinese, it was 13.30 per thousand, both lower than the previous month. The reported births were 55 for foreigners and 111 for Chinese.

Infectious Diseases: Smallpox is usually found when the weather turns cold. There were six cases this month. Diphtheria and scarlet fever were more common in foreigners, but there were no deaths. Scarlet fever was less common in Chinese than in foreigners, and deaths were extremely rare. The number of gastrointestinal cases in foreigners was particularly high. According to the reports of health inspectors, the neglect of general kitchens is a disgrace to civilized people.

Pathological Research: The Pathological Research Laboratory performed 1,824 routine tests, of which 3,996 showed a positive reaction. There were 422 cases related to dysentery. For epidemic prevention work, 1,472 animals were inspected. 59 samples of milk were tested, and 30 samples of tap water were tested, collected from various places within the concession. In addition, 295 chemical analysis tests were performed.

Rabies Treatment: The rabies clinic had 54 patients, of whom 11 came from other cities. 43 of them were advised to receive treatment, 17 completed treatment, 17 were given preventive treatment, and 9 left without completing treatment. A Chinese boy, 11 years old, only came for treatment 17 days after being bitten by a dog. Although he was treated, he eventually died in the isolation hospital.

Vaccination: The vaccination season started on October 1st, and a total of 48,661 people were vaccinated this month. Factory owners who wish to have their workers vaccinated can contact the Health Department, which can work at the factory. Call extension 23 of phone number 12410 for contact.

Food Situation: Milk production increased by more than 4% compared to the previous month. The supply of meat, the number of cattle, sheep, and pigs slaughtered all increased. This is a common phenomenon. More than 17 tons of meat were discarded, and six carcasses were sent to Maohai Road for incineration. The disturbance of tea vendors in various vegetable markets has been cracked down on. 150 cases of violations have been prosecuted. The supply of vegetables is about the same as usual.

Cleaning Work: Vaccination and rat catching work are both quite busy. Many unauthorized thatched sheds were found in the West District and have been removed with the cooperation of the Public Works Department. Canned food with rotten soil was found in a certain auction house. The operation of this type of business must be subject to the restriction of obtaining a license to protect public health.

Applications for Subsidies: Most of the schools that applied for subsidies have been inspected and are generally satisfactory. However, there are also some schools that have not been able to comply despite instructions and guidance. However, what the Health Department requires is the minimum facilities for the health of students.

The National Products Association Introduces Leather Coats and Hats Suitable for Use by Maritime and Aviation Personnel

The Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association believes that this year is the "National Products Year," and factories and craftsmen are working hard to imitate and vigorously produce various new crafts and manufactured goods, which are increasing day by day, making a great contribution to the national movement. However, it is regrettable that the promotion is weak and the publicity is not widespread, making it difficult to achieve the practical effect of universal promotion. The association has been designing relief measures and striving to provide support. In recent days, it has sent personnel to various member factories to conduct on-site investigations and careful assessments. Once the investigation and assessment are completed, if the products are found to be exquisite, beneficial, and practical, the association is responsible for publicizing them in newspapers, introducing them in letters, and promoting the attention of the entire population. This promotes the sales of new national products, in line with the purpose of promoting cooperation between production and sales, and using goods to offset goods. Because the newly produced leather raincoats and hats of the Yuanda Leather Factory meet the needs of people in the maritime and aviation industries, the association sent letters to the Ministry of the Navy and the Aviation Administration yesterday, requesting them to promote and try them out to support national products. The original letter is recorded as follows (omitted above):

Case: Yuanda Leather Factory, a member of our association, stated in a letter that its latest leather coats and hats are soft in texture and novel in style, and are suitable for use by maritime and aviation personnel. Whether it is rain, wind, snow, or severe winter, once worn, the body will warm up, and they are lightweight and comfortable, without hindering work. The camel hair lining, whether leather or single-layer, can be installed and removed at any time, meeting the needs of spring, autumn, and winter. They are especially economical clothing with unique features. At the beginning of the launch, the price is particularly low, but the association is afraid that the publicity is not widespread and the promotion will be difficult to popularize. Therefore, it specifically requested our association to widely introduce them. It is believed that your department has a unique intention in using national products. The products are practical and suitable for actual application. It is appropriate to send a letter to enthusiastically promote and widely adopt them. The national economy and the people's livelihood will benefit greatly.

The Haijingbo Circus Performs a Charity Show to Help with Flood Relief

The Haijingbo Circus has agreed to perform a charity show next Tuesday (the 21st) to help with the Yellow River flood relief. The proceeds from the tickets sold for both the daytime and evening shows on that day will be donated to the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee. This year, the Yellow River has flooded extensively, and those who are in the affected area and have lost their property and have nowhere to go are countless. The Yellow River Flood Relief Committee has been trying its best to rescue the victims. However, relief requires huge sums of money. The committee members consulted with the manager of the Haijingbo Circus, who is known for his philanthropy and good reputation. The circus immediately agreed to sponsor the event. The daytime show on Tuesday will still start at 5:30 PM, and the evening show will start at 9:15 PM. Each performance will have 20 scenes, the same as usual. This is a matter of charity, and it is hoped that the audience will cooperate and come together. This is what the committee and the circus hope for.

The Social Bureau Cracks Down on Deceptive Advertising

The Municipal Social Bureau has found that there are unscrupulous people in the city who are falsely claiming to be foreign firms and using extremely low prices to pre-sell a large number of socially needed goods, water heaters. The proceeds of the sales will be used to organize self-rescue funds, a free one-yuan discount, and a free wool sweater for one yuan per item. After investigation by the personnel sent by the Social Bureau, it was discovered that the advertisements were published by unscrupulous people. The investigation is still ongoing. The Social Bureau received letters from the citizens, asking the Social Bureau to investigate the incidents and to enforce the law severely. The incidents are in accordance with the law of the second clause and fourth item in the advertisement regulation, which dictates that "it is illegal to entice and deceive in order to defraud people of money." The Social Bureau has sent a letter to newspapers to stop these advertisements. The Social Bureau hopes that people in the mainland will learn from their mistakes and not be fooled by such schemes.

Valuable Stolen Goods from Li Yuanhong's Residence in Suzhou Recovered

Suzhou, 16th telegram: A robbery occurred previously at the residence of Li Yuanhong's grandson on Fuxu Road in the British Concession of Shanghai. Chen Shaoquan and other criminals involved in the case were apprehended by the Jing'an Temple Road Patrol and confessed to having hidden some of the stolen goods at the home of Chen Er in 6 Fu Tang, a Suzhou suburb. On the 16th, detectives Wang Lao Wu and two others were dispatched, along with Chen Shaoquan, to Suzhou. They met with detectives Xu Songlin and Wei Guoxiang of the Public Security Bureau and went to Chen Er's home, where they recovered the original stolen goods: a jade ruyi scepter, as well as twelve antique bronze incense burners and other antiques. They were taken back to Shanghai at 7:00 PM, along with the criminal Chen and the stolen goods.

Yaple Factory Replaces Half-Bubble Machine

The Chinese Yaple Electric Appliance Factory, in view of the advancements in modern machinery, and in order to strive for the extraordinary excellence of the factory's products, spared no expense to gradually replace all kinds of machinery in the factory with the latest modern machinery. Zhao Lin's Sentence Reduced After Appeal

Zhao Lin from Shandong, on May 21, 1928, at 9:00 AM, along with the fugitive Jin A San, also known as Wang San, both carrying pistols, broke into Room 19 of the Guangtailai Hotel on Fa Da Ma Road, and shot and killed Liu Yunqi (also known as Shouming) from Guangxi, an official of the Political Training Office of the 33rd Division of the Seventh Army of the National Revolutionary Army. When fleeing, Zhao was caught by Chinese and foreign detectives from the French Concession and sent to the former French Public Concession, where he was sentenced to five years in the Western Prison, and after the term expired, he was sent to the inland government for trial. Zhao served his sentence in prison. In September of this year, after the five-year term expired, Zhao was transferred from the Special No. 2 Prison to the Second Special District Court for review and was sentenced to 18 years in prison for the crimes of jointly conspiring to murder and attempted murder (for shooting and wounding the Western police chief while resisting arrest at the time). Zhao refused to accept the verdict and hired lawyer Zhu Dianqing to file an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The details have been recorded in previous reports. The High Court has completed the trial. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Guo Deting, along with two judges, Sun and Li, opened the court and ruled that the original verdict was revoked, and Zhao Lin was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for joint murder. The number of days spent in custody will be counted as part of the sentence. After the verdict, the appellant was still returned to the detention center to await instructions.

Robbers with Painted Faces Rob Xu Songmao's Family Wealth, Xu's Wife Faints in Bed, Losses of Two to Three Hundred Yuan

Xu Songcang, a resident of No. 33 Chenjiatou in Hongzhen, north of Shanghai, and his son You Sheng, both conduct business in the concession. At home are only Xu's wife, grandson, and daughter-in-law. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, six or seven robbers suddenly arrived. Three robbers held handguns, and two held knives and axes, breaking into the house through the back door. Three or four robbers stood guard outside the door. They first kicked open the door of a tenant, a rural woman, and searched and looted her room. The rural woman earned her living through farming and had no money, foreign clothes, or belongings. The robbers then went to Xu's wife's room to search and loot. Xu's wife, frightened, fainted on the bed, letting the robbers rummage through boxes and chests. In total, clothing and jewelry worth about two to three hundred silver dollars were stolen. As the robbers left, they fired a shot and fled. The location was relatively far from the police station, so the robbers were calm and unhurried. After Xu Songmao received the news and returned home, he checked the lost items and filed a report with the Fifth District's Third Precinct, requesting an investigation. Precinct Chief Wen immediately dispatched Patrol Officer Lin Jing from the Hongzhen sub-station, along with police officers Gao Yucheng, Shen Hongbin, etc., to surround and apprehend the robbers. However, because too much time had passed, the robbers had already fled far away. They returned to Xu's house to investigate. According to Xu's wife, three of the robbers were wearing blue cloth shirts and pants, without hats, and had black ash smeared on their faces, all speaking in a local accent. I was frightened when I saw them, so I fainted on the bed and covered myself with a blanket. According to the tenants, the robbers were carrying handguns about a foot long, all with painted faces. Patrol Officer Lin observed that the robbers were clearly aware that Xu Songmao and his son were not at home, so they painted their faces to commit the robbery. It was undoubtedly done by someone from the vicinity. After completing the investigation, he returned to the station to report and immediately submitted a report to the General Bureau, issuing a general order for coordinated apprehension.

Assistance in Bigamy Case: Both Parties Fail to Appear, Extension of Seven Days Granted

Bi Fengsheng, a native of Changzhou, worked as a plasterer. Three years ago, he married Quan Xiaomei, a woman from Yixing. Xiaomei was of marriageable age and had some beauty. After marrying Bi, they initially lived in harmony. However, because Bi's income was meager and could not afford Xiaomei's extravagant spending, quarrels gradually increased, and their relationship deteriorated. Xiaomei left without notice in January of this year and became involved with Jin Liuzhen. But Jin was a rogue with no stable job or interests, and their life was very difficult. At that time, Gu Quan'gen, a craftsman from Wuxi at the Shuntai Machinery Can Factory at No. 305 Lane Dalian Bay Road, was 23 years old and still single, looking for a woman to marry. Jin Liugen learned of this and colluded with his friends Wu Shaoxian and Qiu Binghua to act as matchmakers. They falsely claimed that Xiaomei was Liugen's younger sister and willing to marry Gu as his wife. They agreed on a bride price of 140 yuan and chose July 17th to hold the wedding at the Taihe Restaurant. Two days after the wedding, Bi Fengsheng, Xiaomei's original husband, learned of this and reported it to the police, who arrested Xiaomei and handed her over to the First Special District Court. The court sentenced Xiaomei to five months in prison for bigamy and sent her to jail. Gu Quangen then hired lawyer Yu Hualong to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court, accusing Wu and Shen of knowingly assisting in bigamy, defrauding and obtaining money, and requesting the court to summon the defendants to court and punish them according to the law, citing Article 254 of the Criminal Law for assisting in bigamy and Article 361 of the same law for defrauding and obtaining money. He also filed a civil lawsuit, demanding that the defendants jointly compensate the plaintiff for the 140 yuan bride price and other losses of over 180 yuan. The court approved the request, and Judge Xue opened a hearing yesterday afternoon. Neither the plaintiff nor the defendant appeared in court. Only the plaintiff's attorney, Yu Hualong, appeared in court and requested an extension. Judge Xue ordered that the case be postponed for seven days for further hearing.

Report on the Reserve for Issuance of the Four Banks Reserve Treasury, No. 202

The Four Banks Reserve Treasury is jointly established by the Yanye, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu banks to exclusively handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank banknotes. According to the treasury's charter, the issuance of banknotes requires full reserves. Cash reserves must be at least 60%, and guarantee reserves must be at most 40%. A public announcement is made every week, and it is reviewed by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. Here is the 202nd announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Treasury on November 11, 22: Value of banknotes in circulation: 26,491,137 yuan. Total reserves: 26,491,137 yuan, including: Cash reserves: 21,068,037 yuan, Guarantee reserves: 5,422,100 yuan.

Letter

To the Editor: I have been instructed by my client, Yin Qiulian, to state that I recently read in today's newspaper an article entitled "Unexpectedly Admits to Being a Citizen of the Puppet State," which is not in accordance with the facts. Qiulian has lived abroad since childhood and is not familiar with the language of this country. Therefore, during the court hearing, she requested the judge to allow her to present her case in English. When the judge asked Qiulian where she was from, Qiulian immediately replied that she was born in Fengtian. However, the word "Munden" was mistakenly translated by the interpreter as Manchuria, leading to a great misunderstanding and error. Qiulian shares the same grief and indignation over the loss of our national territory. She is not insane and would never admit to being a citizen of the puppet state. I am commissioned to correct this statement. Respectfully submitted to the Shen Bao, Lawyers Song Chunfang and Jiang Zongpan, November 16th.

Ministry of Education Invited Ms. Fry to Speak on British Education Yesterday

(Nanjing, 16th dispatch) The Ministry of Education invited British Ms. Fry to give a lecture on British education at 5:00 PM on the 16th. More than 100 people attended, including staff from the Ministry of Education and members of the Sino-British Cultural Association. Minister Wang gave a welcoming speech. Fry said that British education emphasizes autonomy and has now eliminated class concepts. There are two paths to university, and both the poor and the rich can attend. The government encourages donations to support education. In recent years, private schools have sprung up, and funding has increased. Primary and secondary schools have implemented moral education for many years. Religious concepts vary, so educational methods also vary. There is no need to force uniformity. Universities especially emphasize the preservation of each person's unique personality. Tuition fees account for one-tenth or two-tenths of university funding. Government subsidies to universities and private establishments coexist and harmonize with each other. The government does not interfere with university administration due to subsidies to private schools, but the standards for university degrees are very strict. Many university students serve on the faculty, which allows them to interact with teachers. I have observed that Chinese university professors are responsible for educating students, which is very similar to Britain. China's education has recently improved, young people are intelligent, and teachers are well-trained. This impression is the best souvenir I will take with me upon my departure. Wang Shijie believed that Ms. Fry's speech was a good reference for educators in our country and expressed his gratitude. In the evening, the Sino-British Cultural Association hosted a tea party with refreshments to welcome the guests. More than 20 Sino-British members, including Wang Shijie, Shi Ying, and Zhang Daofan, attended, and the guests and hosts enjoyed themselves.

Ministry of Education Issues Order to Correct Arithmetic Time in Elementary School Curriculum

The Ministry of Education issued an order to the Education Bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating: It has been found that the arithmetic time for each grade in the working items of the arithmetic course standard for kindergartens and elementary schools is incorrect. The time for the fourth grade is 240 minutes, and the time for the fifth and sixth grades is 210 minutes, all of which are incorrect by 180 minutes. It is appropriate to urgently send two copies of the errata table for the elementary school arithmetic curriculum time. Please forward it to your subordinates for correction. This order.

The Ministry of Education also issued an order to the Education Bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating: It has been found that the "Regulations for the Amendment of Private Schools" were previously copied and distributed by the Ministry for compliance. Now, it has been found that the word "middle school" in the last paragraph of Article 17 of the previously issued regulations is a printing error for the word "elementary school." It is hereby ordered to be informed and to inform all subordinates to comply. This order.

Student Unrest at Wuben Girls' High School to Be Resolved Soon: Students Have Realized Their Errors and Expressed Their Intent to Resume Classes Soon

The student unrest at the Municipal Wuben Girls' High School has been going on for four days. Yesterday, the situation seemed to be improving. The students have largely accepted the guidance of the faculty and staff. It is expected that the unrest will subside within a day or two. Shanghai News reporters visited various parties yesterday and obtained the following details:

Reasons for Security: Because the school was in a state of disorder after the storm occurred, and entry and exit were unrestricted, the Education Bureau was deeply concerned about male students and other accidents. Therefore, yesterday morning, unarmed police officers were added to the school gate to assist Education Bureau staff in checking entry and exit passes. Later, the school faculty and staff were responsible for maintaining order in the school and continuing to persuade the students. Therefore, at 1:00 PM, the Education Bureau withdrew the police officers.

Results of Persuasion: In the afternoon, representatives of the school's faculty and staff summoned the student grade leaders for a conversation at the school. They earnestly persuaded them. It is heard that the majority of the students have expressed an understanding of their errors. The Education Bureau believes that if the students do not interfere with school administration, classes can resume within a day or two. At that time, the school will notify the parents again. Based on this observation, the student unrest at the school seems to be easily resolved.

Ministry of Education Orders the Issuance of Amended Regulations for Private Schools: Municipal Education Bureau Instructs Private Schools to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction to private schools yesterday, stating: It is hereby notified that the Ministry of Education has issued Instruction No. 10848, which states that the Regulations for Private Schools promulgated by the Ministry in August of the 18th year have now been amended. In addition to being promulgated by the Ministry, it will also be distributed to various provinces. A copy of the amended Regulations for Private Schools is hereby attached for compliance and to instruct your subordinates to comply. This instruction, etc. With this attached, it is found that the procedures for filing a case in accordance with the amended Regulations for Private Schools are simpler than before. However, newly established private schools must comply with the provisions of Article 26, Paragraph 1. Schools that have not been approved by the competent educational administrative authority shall not proceed with enrollment. In the future, if there are newly established schools, they must prepare early and report to the Education Bureau for approval to operate. Only after the Bureau or the Ministry of Education has approved the operation may they advertise for enrollment. Other articles have also been slightly revised. All private schools under your jurisdiction must comply with these regulations. This instruction. The Regulations for Private Schools are published in the 217th issue of the Weekly Report.

Special Item

General Overview of Modern Chinese Education Thought (III) - Narrated by Shu Jincheng - Notes by Sun Yucai - ▲ Factors Contributing to New Educational Thought

If China, eighty years ago, had not experienced the Opium War, even if it had engaged in commerce with foreign countries, I believe it would have been at most a matter of fair trade in the international market. China's social phenomena would definitely not be as they are now, and there would be even less talk of new education. Furthermore, if after the Opium War, the nation had prospered, establishing itself as a world power, if China had not been defeated by Japan, or if the Boxer Rebellion had truly succeeded in driving out the "foreigners," I think China's current education system might still be following the scientific and academy systems that have been passed down for thousands of years. Perhaps some country in the world would even admire the excellence of our nation's system and resolutely imitate it. Truly, the emergence and formation of all systems cannot be separated from the driving force of the environment. The adoption of China's new education system was entirely forced by external forces. In the twenty-eighth year of the Guangxu reign (Qing Dynasty), when Zhang Baixi presented and enacted the Regulations for Schools, he completely abolished the old system in one stroke and transplanted the education system of Western industrial society in its entirety. The fundamental reason for this can be summarized in the four characters "forced by circumstances." In the past sixty years, the emergence of new educational thought in China, while primarily due to international trends, was also jointly promoted by various special backgrounds in our nation's domestic politics, society, world, and academia.

In the past sixty years, China, due to the oppression of international capital imperialism, has suffered from social poverty and financial exhaustion, political fragmentation, and academic plagiarism. Almost nothing is satisfactory. However, within these various unsatisfactory phenomena, there is still a hint of latent progress. This progress is "self-awareness." This widespread self-awareness is truly a characteristic of recent decades. China's survival depends on this self-awareness. In the past sixty years, educational thought, though undergoing various changes due to environmental shifts, is still fundamentally progressing in self-awareness. This is the general principle of modern Chinese educational thought.

▲ History of Changes in Modern Educational Thought Table

Modern educational thought, while moving towards self-awareness, varies greatly in degree. Initially, it was passive and imitative; now, it is active and creative. If we distinguish by time, then the educational thought of the late Qing Dynasty was imitative, while the educational thought since the Republic of China has been self-aware. Within each period, there can be further subdivisions, as shown in the table below.

History of Changes in Modern Chinese Educational Thought

Imitative Period (Qing Dynasty) (Foreign Language Thought, Military Preparation Thought, Western Learning Thought, Western Art Thought, Western Political Thought)

Self-Awareness Period (Republic of China) (Military Nationalism and Military Education Thought, Pragmatism and Practical Thought, Aesthetic Thought, Great Harmony Thought, Vocational Thought, Democratic Governance Thought, Educational Establishment Thought, Scientific Thought, Non-Religious Thought)

(National Thought, Civic Thought, Party-Oriented Thought, Production Education Thought, Rural Education Thought, Mass Education Thought, National Revival Education Thought, Women's Education Thought)

By briefly reviewing the above table, we can understand the general outline of the history of changes in thought. Now, let's delve into the details. For the sake of convenience in explanation, I will specifically divide the many complex thoughts above into five periods for separate explanation.

(I) The "Chinese Learning for Foundation, Western Learning for Application" Period (Opium War to Late Guangxu Reign)

Educational thought changes with social thought and shifts with the trends of the times. This is a consensus we have all reached. After the Opium War, China's various weaknesses were exposed to the outside world. Britain, France, and other countries then came one after another to sign unequal treaties, taking the opportunity to bully us. Consular jurisdiction, equal sharing of benefits, missionary travel, and other matters were all separately stipulated by treaties. As foreigners could freely move deep into the interior, interactions between Chinese and Western peoples became more frequent. Foreigners often relied on the rights granted by unequal treaties, frequently engaging in actions that bullied officials and insulted the people, leading to an increasing number of diplomatic incidents. Because of this, China's educational thought at the time turned entirely towards imitating Westernization. Thus, the saying "Chinese learning for foundation, Western learning for application" became popular. What does this phrase mean? It means using China's inherent culture and scholarship as the foundation and system, while learning and practically applying Western culture and scholarship. It implies promoting Western culture without forgetting the essence of Chinese culture. Naturally, "adopting the strengths of others to compensate for one's own weaknesses" is an eternal principle. Moreover, the situation in our country at the time precisely required Western learning to the extreme. We can divide this period into five aspects for explanation.

▲ Foreign Language Education Thought In the first year of the Tongzhi reign, the Zongli Yamen (Office for Foreign Affairs) recognized that international diplomatic matters were becoming increasingly frequent. Countries such as Britain, France, Russia, America, Sweden, and Norway had successively signed treaties and engaged in commerce. Therefore, it took the lead in advocating the establishment of the Tongwen Guan (School of Combined Learning) in Beijing. Foreign language education thought thus began from this point. In the second year of the Tongzhi reign, Li Hongzhang requested the establishment of the Guangfangyan Guan (School for Broad Language Studies) in Shanghai. In the third year, Ruilin and others also requested the establishment of the Guangdong Tongwen Guan in Guangzhou. All these schools primarily focused on teaching languages and writing. Before the twenty-eighth year of the Guangxu reign, these three schools were truly the institutions of higher education in China's new education system, especially with the Tongwen Guan in Beijing serving as the central hub. Its content can be divided into three major categories: first, cultivating diplomatic talent; second, translating Western books; third, requiring all schools above the secondary level to study foreign languages. Its influences included the emergence of diplomatic talent, the translation of Western and Japanese books, and so on. Later, due to the promotion of missionary schools and the fueling of the student-abroad system, the means gradually became the end.

▲ Military Preparation Education Thought After the Treaty of Nanjing, almost everything was subject to foreign constraints. Statesmen realized that the foreigners' victory over our country was by no means accidental but was backed by their strong armor and sharp weapons. If our country truly wanted to strengthen itself, it would not be enough to simply have diplomatic talent capable of negotiating. It was necessary to "use their ways to deal with their own people." Therefore, after the establishment of the Tongwen Guan and other schools, there followed the emergence of military preparation thought. At the time, the court and the public alike shared a desire for self-strengthening, and their understanding of Western countries focused solely on their strong armor and sharp weapons. Therefore, military preparation became the center of educational thought at the time. Whether it was studying abroad or establishing schools domestically, the goal was invariably to strengthen the military. This thought, starting from the establishment of the Tongwen Guan and lasting until the twenty-eighth year of the Guangxu reign, spanned over forty years. It was truly at its peak, and its influence was not insignificant. For example, establishing military factories, translating Western books, establishing naval and military academies, sending students abroad to specialize in the army, and adding military drills to the curriculum of various schools. The greatest impact was the establishment of the foundation for military nationalist education in modern Chinese educational thought.

▲ Western Learning Education Thought After the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, our country suffered greatly. The entire nation was eager to become stronger as a major task. Therefore, the trend of Western learning flourished for a time. After the Boxer Rebellion in 1900, the implementation of the new education system popularized Western learning throughout the general education circles. Tracing the origins of this thought, the only reason was still foreign aggression. The scope of Western learning initially encompassed astronomy and mathematics. Later, it gradually became more diverse, narrowly referring only to natural sciences and broadly referring to all Western culture. Western learning education thought spanned over sixty years. During these sixty years, almost all aspects of Chinese politics and academics were directly or indirectly influenced by it. The most prominent were: first, the addition of astronomy and mathematics departments to the Tongwen Guan in the fifth year of the Tongzhi reign; second, the various Sino-Western schools established after the Reform Movement of 1898 and before the Boxer Rebellion; third, the science subjects in schools at all levels after the implementation of the new education system; fourth, the absorption of Western culture.

▲ Western Art Education Thought Western art was originally a part of Western learning. After the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, Western learning thought advanced further, and natural sciences and applied sciences were separately established as Western art. Its emergence was also due to the reflection of foreign powers' strong armor and sharp weapons, and its development was due to the lack of practical application in the new education of the late Qing Dynasty. The most important achievements were: first, the recognition of the driving force of Western material civilization; second, the development of industrial schools; third, the gradual breakdown of the concept of "learning for what purpose"; fourth, the extension from recognizing the advantages of Western technology to valuing Western skills. It is a pity that most of the facilities for establishing industrial schools and studying abroad were merely empty words. Therefore, for decades, China's technology did not make any significant progress due to Western art education thought.

▲ Western Political Education Thought After our country was influenced by the Japanese Meiji Restoration, everyone knew that Western learning contained extremely complex elements. Therefore, a part of the arts and skills was named Western art, and a part of politics was called Western politics. After Western art and Western politics were separated, Western political education received special attention from the people. Because at the beginning of the reform, everything was waiting to be done. Without talented and decisive leaders in political talent, almost everything would be difficult to accomplish, and there was no way to talk about skills. However, Western political education thought was very short-lived, lasting only for more than ten years from the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895 to the end of the Qing Dynasty. In its positive aspects, its greatest impact was: first, the absorption of Western culture; second, the establishment of the Republic of China. Therefore, the practical impact of Western political education was indeed very significant. At the same time, it also bore a particularly large responsibility for the various negative phenomena in Chinese politics and society for decades.

Spring and Autumn

The Whip

— Xianxian

Anyone who has seen a Hae Chin Po circus probably won't forget the whip that can be used to demonstrate power and subdue dragons and tigers.

Wild beasts, no matter how tamed, can never escape their wild nature. Although willing to work hard, wild beasts are willing to work for their masters, but sometimes they can become feral and make trouble for their masters, refusing to perform. But when they hear the master crack the whip in his hand, emitting one or two strange sounds that make the hair stand on end, they will naturally obey the master's command with their heads bowed.

Thus, I have developed a great admiration for the whip. Maintaining order requires the whip. Not only are whips necessary for wild beasts, but also for people to people, and even more so for civilized people to barbaric peoples. However, people use a formal "whip" for wild beasts, while people use the spirit of the "whip" or a means beyond the "whip" for each other.

Black slaves, in the eyes of white people, are no different from the wild beasts in a circus. To maintain order among blacks, a whip should be in hand, otherwise, blacks will surely become feral and disturb the peace of whites. Therefore, although blacks have been liberated, "blacks" are ultimately different from "whites."

It is not just that blacks are different from whites. All colored people in the world, except for Japan, should be subjected to a few whips from the white race. Therefore, the United States invented the Monroe Doctrine, Africa was divided among several European powers, and six or seven tenths of Asia is also dealt with by white people who have means beyond the "whip" to deal with colored people who have evolved from wild beasts.

The maintenance of peace in East Asia must naturally be attributed to the whip of the Japanese Empire. Indeed, in East Asia, there is a great sleeping lion that has never roared. If this great sleeping lion wants to open its eyes, in order to maintain peace in East Asia, the whip in the master's hand will emit strange sounds to command it to sleep. In recent days, the whip that commands the sleeping lion has also been moved to train a European bear. I wonder if the next great circus can sell out again in Geneva.

Victim

— Tongchu

This morning, before I even washed my face, a school servant brought news: "A baby has been abandoned on the wall across the street." What does a discarded baby look like? Driven by curiosity, I dragged a colleague along, even though I hadn't washed my face.

In a metropolis, this is not considered a rare event; but after all, it is a child, after all, it is an abnormal act, abandoning one's own child. A crowd had already gathered, and when I saw the "abandoned baby," my chest felt a severe pressure, and I was breathing heavily.

Wrapped in red swaddling clothes, his small face was revealed in the white felt; his eyes were closed, his mouth did not move, and his face was flushed. I didn't know if it was the tension of the blood after his cries, or a symbol of what is called a blood child. Those who watched did not say a word, and I only heard the faint sound of tongues and teeth moving: "Tsk! Tsk! Tsk! Tsk!" filling the air, creating a terrible and strange scene. In this situation, there are at least two things that deserve our attention.

First. The key to women's liberation is that chastity is still the second life of women in today's society. Otherwise, would the mother of the abandoned baby have the heart to abandon him? Women's liberation, demanding freedom and equality, has been chanted for a long time, and on the surface, everything has been achieved. But the facts show us that, except for a few, who does not depend on men? Because they depend on men, there are such heartbreaking things. Therefore, true women's liberation still needs to find a foothold economically.

Second. Sexual life urgently needs to be improved properly. Few people talk about this issue, as if it is not worth mentioning. But the facts are there. The matter of seeking pleasure in brothels has been countless throughout history. The authority of the law cannot suppress them, and society and public opinion cannot subdue them, giving them more victories and sacrificing their crystallization. Alas! That crystallization is not a private thing, the sacrifice is still social. Hereafter, I deeply hope that enlightened people will study it and find a proper way to improve it.

X X X

Crying for Uncle Yi

— Shouou

One day after the Double Ninth Festival, a friend from the French Concession came and told me, "Your uncle, Mr. Yiqing, has passed away!" When I heard this, I lowered my head and said nothing. The friend repeated, "He passed away more than a month ago! Don't you know?" I still said nothing, because I didn't know what to say. After a long time, I began to say, "I suppose it was because the family had just moved that I didn't receive the news. But I already knew that he would not be willing to linger in this muddy world. Now that I hear what you say, it matches what I expected, so it's not surprising, but my heart is still inevitably heavy."

Uncle Yi's surname was Wu, his given name was Zonglian, and Yiqing was his style name. In the late Qing Dynasty, he was once an envoy to Italy, Britain, and France, and was a predecessor in our country's diplomatic circles. I suppose many people know him.

However, in addition to being proficient in English and French, my uncle rarely had the demeanor of today's diplomats. His words and actions were extremely sincere, like a village scholar. Therefore, although he traveled as an official for more than ten years, reaching the highest rank, his purse remained as tight as ever. However, when relatives and friends asked for help, he would not hesitate to reduce his own expenses to help them. Later, after he retired from official life, there were those who came to him for help. Although he had nothing to give, he still tried his best to find ways, not shying away from hard work and complaints. Whenever someone asked him to be a guarantor, he would agree without hesitation, so he was often implicated and had to repay debts for others. However, after only a few days, he would be a guarantor for someone else. I once heard him say, "People would not be willing to disregard their reputation and burden the guarantor unless they had no choice. When they asked me to be a guarantor, they did not intend to burden me, so how can I refuse them!" His loyalty and kindness were like this.

Uncle also liked to act like Cao Qiu, helping relatives and party members who were unemployed, even if they did not ask him. However, those in power today are mostly snobbish. Even if they had a deep friendship with Uncle in the past, they now know that he has lost power. Therefore, people who hold letters from Uncle to visit officials rarely succeed. When Uncle heard about this, he would angrily exclaim, "Human feelings are thinner than autumn clouds!"

In recent years, my uncle has been too enthusiastic. He has paid too much for others, and his finances have become extremely tight. Those who are unworthy often fabricate rumors and ridicule him in various ways, even making things difficult for him to his face. Therefore, the old man's hidden pain deepened day by day, and his spirit gradually weakened. Now he is indeed gone! But he lived to be over ninety years old, which is a blessing from heaven to a kind and honest person, not something that could be achieved by taking ginseng and deer velvet every day.

The Heart of the Chinese

— Yan Bokuang

I remember seeing F'kiein's "The Heart of the Chinese" in a certain Western magazine. He said: "The heart of the Chinese is obviously different from that of Westerners: (1) They have no creative mind, (2) They harbor a fluke mentality, (3) They have no patriotism, (4) They harbor a destructive mind." The way he said it was as if he had X-ray glasses on his eyes, seeing through the crux of the matter. But do we Chinese really have the above mentality? Readers might as well think about it!

(1) No Creative Mind: Chinese people indeed have no creative mind. For example, people in business, seeing that someone else's business is good, immediately start doing the same business. If someone's writing is good, they immediately imitate or plagiarize.

(2) Harboring a Fluke Mentality: We can definitely say that we have this weakness. For example, now you can get a bonus for smoking cigarettes, you can get a bonus for using soap... Not only do foreigners use this weakness of ours! Even the Chinese themselves are using themselves, to the point that everyone has developed a mentality of getting something for nothing, which is truly lamentable!

(3) No Patriotism: This cannot be generalized. In such a large China, among the 450 million people, there must be many people who have patriotism, right? However, seeing that the import of enemy goods does not decrease, it can be known that there must be many people who have no patriotism, so although this year is National Goods Year, national goods still cannot sell well.

(4) Harboring a Destructive Mind: When someone is doing something, they are secretly sabotaging it, or someone has painted a snow-white wall, but children go and draw marks on it, or someone has posted a wall advertisement, but vandals tear it down. This is harboring a destructive mind, which is also lacking a sense of morality.

Therefore, I hope that readers, after seeing my writing, realize that we Chinese do have this phenomenon, then persuading others everywhere would also be a good thing.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eighteen - Tea with Tender Feelings to Comfort the Couple - Hasty Departure with Forced Smiles to Bid Farewell to Family

He was afraid there wouldn't be enough time, so he immediately blew his whistle and gathered all the soldiers of the company in the courtyard. After calling the roll, seeing a company of brothers standing in front of him, he thought to himself, these people are all going to the outside of the Great Wall to fight for their lives, and in this division of people, this doesn't count as a big deal, but as far as each individual is concerned, it is the biggest thing they will ever do in their lives. How can we let them go on the road confused without saying a word? But thinking about the days when he was a soldier, when he was about to leave, which battalion commander had ever mentioned anything? If he were to say something, wouldn't that be meddling? So he simply didn't say a word. After standing in formation, he led the brothers to the battalion headquarters for assembly, and then from the battalion headquarters to the parade ground. The sun in the eastern sky, like a golden basin, cast golden sunlight onto the parade ground, shining on Zhao Ziqiang's regiment standing with their backs to the sun. Their regimental commander, from afar, said a few words of instruction without reason, and then asked loudly, "Brothers, have you eaten your fill?" Everyone drew a breath from their dan tian and replied, "We've eaten our fill!" He asked again, "Have you had your fill of drinks?" They all replied in unison, "We've had our fill!" Then Battalion Commander Bao Fang personally came out and shouted the command, "Right turn, forward march!" They were the first battalion, so naturally they were walking at the front of the regiment. Zhao Ziqiang followed the team, walking step by step along the Shanghai Dian Avenue. If he hadn't been following the team, he wouldn't have known where he was going or where he was walking. The marching troops were not walking too busily. The brothers were walking at a comfortable pace, one foot high and the other low. Some were talking quietly in twos and threes, and some were singing very softly. Zhao Ziqiang thought to himself, the brothers are all setting out calmly, so why am I so distraught? So he straightened his chest and looked straight ahead, walking step by step. (242)

World News

Italians Promote Fashion Trends

Italy has also heard of panic in recent years, but Italian industrialists, following Mussolini's guidance, not only love to use domestic goods and revive foreign trade, but they also go to Paris as the center of the world's Hua industry and the source of world fashion. Therefore, clothing stores in Italian metropolises such as Milan and Florence have vigorously launched new styles, even suppressing Parisian speculators. Therefore, the world's great tycoons have all rushed to Italy upon hearing the news.

French Lifespan

In recent years, the lifespan of French people has gradually increased. Since the French Revolution, the average lifespan has been only 28 years and 9 months. By 1800, it had increased to 40 years, in 1900 to 45 years and 9 months, and in 1910 to 48 years. Although there were no accurate statistics during the war, the average age between 1920 and 1932, for Paris alone, was 52 years and 3 months for men and 56 years for women. In 1911, there were only 13,901 elderly people over the age of 80 living in Paris, with women twice as many. By 1926, there were 16,671 men over the age of 80, and the number of women had doubled. According to last year's statistics, the number of deaths was 13.6 per thousand, which is a very significant decrease compared to 1909.

Minister's Daughter

Hungarian Finance Minister Baron Golan's daughter, Branci Yuan, is 20 years old this year. Because she is studying home economics, she went to a coffee shop near the old palace of Putabespiside to learn how to make chicken cakes and ice cream. She studies for six hours every day. People think that the daughter of the minister is willing to look for a job, so the daughters of other powerful people also thought of the job front.

Korean Lifespan

In places with cold climates, people's lifespans, according to statistics released by the Italian Statistics Bureau, are 55 years and 3 months for Norwegians, 55 years for Swedes, 53 years for Dutch, 50 years and 5 months for British, 47 years for Belgians, 47 years for French, 46 years for Germans, 44 years for Italians, and 41 years for Austrians. According to this, Norway is the coldest country in Europe, and its lifespan is the longest, while Austria is the hottest country, and its lifespan is the shortest. It can be seen that from cold to warm, the lifespan gradually decreases.

Encouraging Soldiers to Drink

The Hungarian army is the most fond of drinking in the world. They have to drink some Tuja wine almost every day, but Tuja wine is very expensive, and they cannot buy as much as they want after all. General Gongbo, the Chief of the Army, heard that the soldiers did not have money to drink Tuja wine, so he proposed a capital of 240,000 yuan to subsidize Tuja wine manufacturers, ordering them to improve the quality of the wine and reduce the price of the wine. In particular, the price must be especially cheap for the soldiers, so the Hungarian soldiers are very grateful for the good intentions of the Chief of the Army, so that they can drink freely.

Lions Also Lose Jobs

The Paris City Authority is now unable to cope with the unemployment problem of a hundred lions.

These lions initially participated in the German circus and patrolled in various European countries. Later, the circus disbanded, and the lions were sent back to Paris. The city authority wanted to temporarily deposit the lions in the zoo, but the zoo did not have a budget for raising lions, and there was no place to place the lions, so it refused to deposit them. Now, a hundred lions are in a situation where they cannot be disposed of, so they have to post an advertisement for cheap sale. It is said that until now, there are really not many employers.

Grain: Factory Inventory Low, Tag Flour Rebounds

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, each month presented a stable and strong appearance. Although foreign wheat quotations in Chicago were about six jiao lower, and Canadian small ones were about one point lower, the market sentiment remained stable after the opening. Although there was dumping of foreign wheat, it could not become a reality at present. Moreover, since the inventory of each factory was searched by the northern gangs, it was no longer substantial. Therefore, the sentiment of outsiders was extremely firm, and people inside and outside the industry paid great attention to it. And because of the short covering of inland manufacturers, the market atmosphere gradually stabilized. When the afternoon market opened, because the morning did not fall but rose, the market sentiment became more firm, and the near term was getting better and better due to the Tianjin gangs' purchase. The long term also presented a strong image because there were not many sales. Looking at the future situation, such as the lack of inventory, it is feared that there will be a good side. As a result, this month rebounded by three fen and seven li and a half, December rose by two fen and two li and a half, January rose by fen, February rose by one fen and a half, March rose by one fen and two li and a half, and April rose by one fen and a half.

However, market sentiment was that although there were continued successes in foreign wheat, the domestic arrivals in the near term were not visible, and the market situation thereafter must be stabilized. Therefore, although transactions were not smooth, market sentiment was very firm.
